Current Commentary

After Overcoming Fuzhou, [Regarding] 元

This campaign to conquer Fujian: Yanping was captured, Gutian was taken, Xiamen was recovered, and now there is even talk of the navy conquering Fuzhou. Whether this is true remains to be seen, but the expectation is likely not far off. However, after Fuzhou is conquered, will the military campaign conclude there, or will the victory be used to advance and quell the entire province's Fujian army? As we see it, the military action may conclude there. Why? Because this military campaign in Fujian province is different from other internal wars. It is a so-called "last resort." Using military force as a last resort only seeks to subdue them and stop there. It is a so-called "compassionate restraint, not rejoicing," unlike other wars to seize cities and land. Capturing a city and gaining a territory is not to show off the strength of our military power, boast about the glory of our military achievements, and take advantage of the victory to advance until everything is as we desire. At the beginning of the Fujian Incident, the 19th Route Army relied on the battle of January 28th, thinking they could get lucky once again. Now that they have suffered this major blow, it is only natural that they will become aware and develop a sense of regret. At this point, the central government should stop at the appropriate time, giving them an opportunity to repent and avoid pursuing them like cornered bandits. Since the use of military force was a last resort, if there are other ways to resolve the matter besides military force, then we should seek them through other means. Moreover, there are many disputes regarding political issues in addition to military matters, and they cannot all be resolved by military force. Therefore, the Fujian campaign must begin with military force but end with peace. Furthermore, we have something more to say: the outbreak of this Fujian Incident is just one issue among many. If the central government can handle this Fujian Incident appropriately, it can reduce the discontent and resentment of others who are dissatisfied with the central government. We say this not because the central government's military victory this time is enough to subdue them, but because the central government can take this opportunity to resolve the Fujian affair and implement its stated commitment to unity and transparency in everything. According to reports, central figures have consistently expressed a willingness to fully accept the Southwest's demands and Mr. Hu Hanmin's eight proposals. If the authorities genuinely and thoroughly demonstrate this desire for openness as the Fujian affair comes to a close, making it clear to all parties that the government is not biased towards any one party and genuinely intends to recruit talents from outside the party, then success will be easier than when the Fujian Incident first broke out. Why is this so? Because if we talked about cooperation and unity when the Fujian Incident first broke out, people would suspect that the central government was forced to do so because it had no other choice, and that it might not be genuinely sincere in cooperating and uniting. After the recovery of Fuzhou, people will suspect that the central government will suddenly change its face because of its military victory, cancel its previous intentions for unity and cooperation, and replace it with an authoritarian attitude. Although this kind of speculation is close to judging a gentleman with the heart of a petty person, it is still within the realm of general human nature. Now, if the central government can demonstrate, after its military victory, that the use of military force was a last resort, and quickly use peaceful means to resolve the Fujian situation, without prolonging the disputes and causing the people to suffer more from the pain of war, and at the same time sincerely adhere to the original intention of cooperation and unity, earnestly seeking a way to save the country with the Southwest and making the path public to show the way of impartiality and selflessness, then people's previous suspicion that the central government had no other choice and only spoke of cooperation and unity can be dispelled. The later suspicion that the central government would rely on its victory and only advocate military force can also be completely resolved. This is why we say that success will be easier.

Alas, the affairs of the country are difficult, and have reached an extreme. The people who hold the reins of power, a single thought, a single action, affects the whole country. Mussolini, Hitler, and others were able to endure hardships and cope with changes in the world because of their sincere intentions, which inspired their people to move towards spiritual unity. The world has never seen a country that can face external challenges when it is not united internally, nor has it seen a country that can unify its people by relying solely on military force. As the Fourth Plenary Session is about to open, our government should quickly rise up and address this.

Xia Ziming's Troops Arrive in Xuanhua and Return to Qin Dechun's Command, To Be Reorganized; Liu Guitang Leads Remnants Back to Qingliu and Shen County

(Beiping) After Xia Ziming led his troops to break away from Liu Guitang, on the 9th of this month, all of them arrived in Xuanhua as ordered to await orders. Xia's troops still have two infantry regiments, mostly elite troops from Liu's army, with well-equipped firearms. Song Jue decided to assign these troops to Qin Dechun for command. Qin plans to return to Chahar in two or three days and will inspect the troops in a special train in Xuanhua to reorganize them. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Beiping) After the bandit Liu's troops fled south from the suburbs of Beiping to southern Hebei, a portion of them gathered in Gu'an, along with more than a thousand local bandits, totaling more than two thousand, and occupied Shuangtang Town east of Xincheng. Another group of seven or eight hundred fled to Kougang Town southwest. Most of them fled into Ba County on the morning of the 5th of this month, crossed Xincheng again, and fled south to Xiong County. On the 8th, they crossed the river at Niangniang Temple southeast of Xiong County and fled to Liangzhaoying northeast of Renqiu. Because He Zhuguo and Xu Tingyao's armies were stationed south of the Pinghan Railway, with strong forces, the bandits did not succeed, so on the 10th, they turned south to the Jinpu Railway, attempting to escape back to their old nest in Shandong Province. After Han's troops intercepted them, a portion of them dispersed into Shandong Province. Liu himself led two thousand bandits and retreated to Qingyuan and Shen County in southern Hebei on the 12th, planning to flee to Henan Province via southern Hebei. He Zhuguo's troops stationed in southern Hebei have dispatched teams to actively pursue and suppress them. At the same time, Pang Bingxun and other troops stationed in northern Henan are also preparing to intercept them. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Beiping) The remnant bandits of Liu have fled to the deep mountains around Baodugang in southern Shandong. Liu plans to temporarily hide there, slightly reorganize, and then flee across the Yellow River to western Henan in six groups. Cui Erdan's nephew, Bangjie, serves as a brigade commander in Liu's army. Bangjie had contacted Erdan beforehand. Liu's attempt to flee to western Henan this time is to join forces with Erdan. After the Hebei authorities received the report, they dispatched teams to strictly guard the Daming area and telegraphed Liu Zhi to prevent the troops from crossing the river. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Jinan) Han Fuqu stated that Liu Guitang's troops once fled to the junction of Daming and Pu County yesterday. Because the provincial army blocked them, they have now fled back to the vicinity of Daming. Hengshui and Xian County still have remnants. He has now appointed a certain division commander as the commander of the western Shandong garrison, leading troops to prevent them. (Special dispatch on the 12th)

(Jinan) Han stated that Shandong Province has strictly prevented Liu Guitang from fleeing south. Zhan Shutang's division opened Pu County Guancheng. Li Hanzhang's division and the second route of the cavalry regiment, the Ru regiment, are in charge of northern Shandong. The Yellow River has not yet frozen, and the boats are all on the south bank. It is difficult for Liu's troops to fly across. He has no need to go to northern Shandong for the time being. He also telegraphed both Chairmen Yu and Liu that Liu's troops have no territorial restrictions. Zhan's division has already crossed the river west from Changqing. Also, the people in Jing County, Nangong, and Zaoqiang are fleeing to Dezhou. Liu's troops are still in Wuyi and Hengshui. Liu himself is in Heng. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

(Beiping) After Xia Ziming led his troops to break away from Liu Guitang, he has been ordered to arrive in Xuanhua. Customs Treasury Bonds for the 23rd Year Will Be Issued This Month, Underwritten by Various Banks (Nanjing)

The Ministry of Finance, due to the large number of loans from banks over the years, will issue 100 million yuan of customs treasury bonds for the 23rd year to repay the accumulated debts. These treasury bonds are purely for repaying previous outstanding loans and will not be circulated on the market. They are underwritten by various banks at 98. Minister Kong has already negotiated with various banks and the issuance will take place this month. The face value is divided into 100 yuan, 1,000 yuan, and 10,000 yuan, with a monthly interest rate of 5%. Principal and interest will be repaid monthly, starting from the date of issuance, and will be fully repaid in seven years, until December of the 29th year of the Republic of China. The Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will be the institutions for repaying principal and interest. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

The Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Finance Will Continue to Discuss Ways to Recover Merchant Stock Advances from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (Nanjing)

According to the Ministry of Communications, when the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company initially recovered merchant stocks, the company's funds were insufficient, so Zhu Jiahua of the Ministry of Communications and former Minister of Finance Song Ziwen agreed that the Central Bank would advance funds for recovery. It was also decided that the advanced funds did not need to be repaid by the company in order to expand shipping services. However, in December of last year, the Central Bank suddenly demanded repayment of the advanced funds from the company. The company then submitted a report to the Ministry and the Executive Yuan, requesting that all advanced funds be allocated to the company as capital. Subsequently, the Executive Yuan handed the matter over to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Communications for consultation. After one meeting, the issue remained unresolved. The Ministry of Communications intends to request the government to approve the allocation of 15 million from the National Economic Council's capital to the company, with the Ministry of Finance deducting the amount advanced by the Central Bank to complete the formalities. It is now planned to hold another consultation within the next week to reach a final resolution. (Special dispatch on the 13th)

Japan's Hegemonic Ambitions: Preparing to Withdraw from the Naval Treaty to Lay the Groundwork for Demanding a Change in Ratios; the United States Opposes, Having Already Expressed Various Views; After Ten Years of Peace, a Great Storm Will Be Stirred Up Again; the Situation in the Pacific Will Cause Disputes Between Italy and France

(London) According to reliable sources, the Japanese government plans to comply with the provisions of the Washington Naval Treaty and issue a two-year advance notice of withdrawal from the treaty. This is because Japan is determined to expand its navy, roughly intending to make its strength equal to that of Britain and the United States. (National Telegram on the 13th)

(Washington) The State Department and the Navy Department stated today that the US government was not surprised to hear that Japan intended to terminate the Washington Naval Limitation Treaty. Washington has not yet received an official statement on this matter, but messages received last year have confirmed that Japan intends to demand an increase in its naval ratio after 1936. Japan wants its fleet to be equal to that of Britain and the United States, instead of the 5:5:3 ratio. The US government has long regarded it as a major issue to be discussed at the 1935 Naval Limitation Conference. Japan's notice of intention to terminate the treaty two years later is to prepare the ground for making demands when the conference is convened in 1935 to discuss the continuation or amendment of the treaty. Washington has already expressed various views that the United States is determined to oppose Japan's increasing its naval ratio. The reason is that Japan's navy does not need to be equal as long as the Pacific trust territories are not fortified and cannot be used to attack Japan. Several senior naval officers, especially those of the big navy faction, were quite pleased to hear the news that Japan would issue the notice, believing that this would provide a better opportunity to request huge sums of money to build warships and aircraft in the next two years. General observers see Japan's proposed notice to abolish the treaty as a major issue for the navy. After ten years of naval peace, there will be more troubles from this. They are deeply afraid that the situation in the Pacific may become a major issue for France and Italy to disagree on naval equality. (National Telegram on the 13th)

Regarding Japan as a Hypothetical Enemy, the Soviet Far East Air Force Makes Rapid Advances, Approaching the Level of Advanced Aviation. Brief Overview of the Performance of Three Types of Aircraft

According to Japanese news, regarding Japan as a hypothetical enemy, the Soviet Union has been focusing on strengthening its Far East military since the Manchurian Incident. By using the Maritime Province as a base, Japan's Sakhalin, Hokkaido, Honshu, Kyushu, and Korea are all within bombing range, which they consider to be a valuable asset. In their war plan against Japan, they have adopted an air force-centric strategy, creating a vast air fleet to compensate for the inferiority of their navy. According to recent information received by the Japanese military, the Soviet Air Force has made extraordinary progress. The number of imported goods rapidly declined in 1933, and in 1934, the first line of the Soviet Air Force was equipped with sophisticated, purely domestically produced military aircraft, which is a noteworthy fact. Particularly noteworthy is that the performance of these domestically produced, first-line military aircraft, divided into bombers, fighters, and reconnaissance aircraft, has improved remarkably, approaching the level of advanced aviation countries such as Britain, France, and Germany. The performance of the three types of aircraft is briefly outlined below:

TB-2 Heavy Bomber

This aircraft is designed with the goal of actively attacking Japan, with a particular emphasis on range. It can carry 16 personnel and is equipped with four domestically produced M-17 600-horsepower engines. The maximum speed is 240 kilometers per hour, and the endurance is 14 hours. It has excellent performance. If it were to attack Tokyo from Vladivostok, it could reach Tokyo airspace in five hours, with approximately five hours of bombing and aerial combat capability remaining.

I-7 Fighter

This is an improved version of the Soviet Air Force's elite I-5 from last year. It has a speed of 300 kilometers per hour and is equipped with a domestically produced M-22 700-horsepower engine. The maximum speed is actually 305 kilometers per hour. It can fly between Tokyo and Osaka in one hour. As a fighter emphasizing speed, it can be considered the world's best.

R-6 Reconnaissance Aircraft

This aircraft is a two-seater equipped with a domestically produced M-34 800-horsepower engine. The maximum speed is 240 kilometers per hour, and the endurance is approximately seven hours. Its value in aerial combat as a medium-range reconnaissance aircraft is the focus of attention from all parties. (World News Agency)

Stalin Discusses with American Reporter the Greatest Crisis Between Soviet Russia and Japan, the Responsibility Lies Entirely with the Japanese Military Clique

Moscow - Joseph Stalin, General Secretary of the Soviet Communist Party, who holds the entire political power of Soviet Russia, recently made the following important remarks to the Moscow correspondent of the New York Times:

The restoration of diplomatic relations between Soviet Russia and the United States opens a path for mutual cooperation, which is most gratifying politically and economically. Soviet Russia can import more foreign goods, but it is unwilling to issue orders if it cannot afford to pay. Therefore, we do not want to import foreign goods on one side without being able to export our goods on the other. We will not stop paying. As with other countries, some say that Soviet Russia has no ability to pay, which is a big mistake, because we have never stopped paying.

Our most ardent wish is to maintain friendship with Japan, but we cannot do this alone. As long as Japan adopts a friendly policy towards Soviet Russia, cooperation between the two countries will not be a problem. However, we deeply worry that the Japanese military clique will oppose a friendly policy, which is the greatest crisis between the two countries.

We do not want the crisis to come, but we cannot but prepare to deal with it. If a country is exposed to danger and its government does not try to defend itself, it will inevitably be abandoned by the people. We do not think it wise for Japan to attack us. Japan's economic situation is not very favorable. It has "Manchukuo" and China as its neighbors, but if it goes to war with Soviet Russia, which country will be its backer? A good soldier is not always a good economist.

We expect to eventually conclude a trade agreement with Britain, but under the current circumstances, whether it can be concluded soon is a question.

Italy has not made any proposals to us regarding the reorganization of the League of Nations.

Soviet Russia's biggest problem at present is to improve its system of supplying goods to cities and villages, and to improve its transportation system, especially the railways. These problems are not easy to solve, but since we have overcome even greater difficulties in the past, we are confident that we can eventually solve these difficulties in the future. The problem of industrialization has now been solved, and the problem of collective agriculture has also been solved. The only problems that remain to be solved are to improve the system of supplying goods and the transportation system. (World News Agency)

In addition to detailing Austria's various loans and analyzing Austria's budget, the report concludes that Austria's monetary credit has regained stability, capital flowing out of the country is gradually returning to the country, the economic reorganization movement has been underway for more than a year and has now stopped, all aspects have improved considerably, unemployment is gradually decreasing, and foreign trade is more active than in 1932. (Havas, 13th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Financial Committee has begun reviewing the report on Bulgaria's financial situation, which states that Bulgaria's finances have shown improvement for the first time since the global economic panic. There are two reasons for this: (1) a good harvest; (2) the foreign trade and exchange supervision policies implemented by the National Bank are well-suited to local needs. (Havas, 12th)

French Senate Discusses Foreign Policy Issues

(Paris) The Senate met today to discuss foreign policy issues. Senator Ambrest spoke, saying that France has always trusted international treaties, but now it is disappointed. The sacrifices France has made to Germany have also been in vain. France originally had infinite hope for the League of Nations, but Germany turned its back on it, and Italy attacked it as well. In addition, the Locarno Treaty has been abandoned, and the Four-Power Pact is intended by Mussolini as a tool to revise the peace treaties, which is extremely dangerous in nature. As for the Disarmament Conference, it has failed to disarm and has instead become a conference for controlling rearmament. Reymilly then gave a speech recounting the history of diplomacy after the European War, stating, "Germany is determined to remove all restraints. We must not reduce the country's strength again this time." He concluded, "France should no longer adopt a labor-saving policy. The people should strictly observe discipline and fulfill their obligations. The government should lead the people to enter this path," and so on. Next, Poulet addressed the meeting, first saying that Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour's unwillingness to greatly reform the League of Nations was very satisfying. He then said that the Four-Power Pact was a good thing because it eased the atmosphere between the two countries. Finally, he said that Britain cannot remain isolated. Senator Hubert then spoke, saying that the alliances created by the European War should not be abandoned and that all misunderstandings that may arise should be eliminated. The meeting was then adjourned, to be continued next Tuesday. (Havas, 12th)

Roosevelt Approves Alcohol Tax Bill

△ Annual Revenue Increase of 500 Million Yuan

Another Step in the Government's Financial Policy

Preparing to Take Over Gold Reserves from Reserve Banks

(Washington) President Roosevelt today approved the alcohol tax bill. This bill stipulates that distilled spirits will be taxed at two dollars per gallon, beer at five dollars per barrel, and other alcoholic beverages at four cents to forty cents per gallon, depending on the alcohol content. Beverages with an alcohol content exceeding 24 percent will be treated as distilled spirits and taxed at two dollars per gallon. It is estimated that this bill will generate 500 million yuan in revenue annually. (Reuters, 12th)

(Washington) It is still unknown what actions President Roosevelt will take regarding gold in the future. Attorney General Cummings has presented to the President his opinion on whether the government can immediately take over the gold reserves of the Federal Reserve without waiting for Congress to pass a bill. Judging from the situation, President Roosevelt seems to want to take over the reserves of the various Reserve Banks so that the gold surplus denominated in dollars can be attributed to the government. President Roosevelt believes that he has the right to take it over, but President Roosevelt has not yet announced his plan. Therefore, it is still uncertain whether President Roosevelt will take over the reserves of the Reserve Banks worth 3.6 billion yuan. (Reuters, 12th)

New Uses for Silver

Important Discoveries in the Medical Field

(London) Dr. Shelton of England has discovered the important functions of silver in the human body and certain plants. It is claimed that the most silver is found in the adrenal glands and the tonsils, especially in childhood. Therefore, young children lacking silver often have the habit of putting silver coins in their mouths. In plants, the growth of pennycress and nicotine, and the secretion of tobacco trichomes, also benefit from silver. According to this invention, which was announced today in the British Medical Journal, silver has the potential for new uses and can provide a basis for silver advocates to increase their arguments. British Senators Pittman and Thomas will definitely pay attention to this. (Reuters, 13th)

French Giant Swindle Case Sparks Fierce Debate, Paris Returns to Calm. Chaudemps Wins Vote of Confidence. House of Representatives Passes Government Trust Vote. Decision on Swindle Case to be Thoroughly Investigated by the Courts. Interesting Drama of Former Prime Ministers' Verbal Sparring

(Paris) Paris is now calm again, and the Chaudemps Cabinet has regained stability, as the House of Representatives tonight passed a vote of confidence in the government by a vote of 376 to 205. The result of the two days of fierce debate in the House of Representatives regarding the Bayonne swindle case was a personal victory for Prime Minister Chaudemps. The motion to form a parliamentary investigation committee has failed, and the judiciary can now carry out its duties without political interference. Chaudemps strongly opposed the motion to form an investigation committee proposed by the right-wing party, because the Stavisky swindle case is purely judicial in nature and has nothing to do with politics. This motion was ultimately defeated by a vote of 360 to 229.

Case for Establishing an Investigative Committee Rejected Due to Delays

(Paris) This afternoon, the House of Representatives continued to discuss the interpellation regarding the Stavisky swindle case. Right-wing parliamentarian Ybarnégaray proposed appointing 44 members of the House of Representatives to form an investigative committee to handle the swindle case. As a result, the House of Representatives rejected it by a vote of 360 to 229, still expressing confidence in the government. The details of the discussion are recorded below: When Parliamentarian Ybarnégaray spoke, he mentioned the Hungarian bond affair. Finance Minister Bonnet replied that the Bank for International Settlements had never guaranteed Stavisky. Stavisky originally intended to sell these bonds in France, and he (Bonnet claimed) obtained the consent of Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour and forbade it. Otherwise, the amount Stavisky swindled would probably be more than it is now, at least an additional 500 million francs. Ybarnégaray then accused former Labor Minister Dalimier, saying that since he had allowed the Social Insurance Bank to subscribe to Bayonne municipal bonds, why had he not investigated Stavisky and Tissier, the director of the Bayonne Municipal Credit Bank, who were involved in this matter in advance? Isn't that a bit negligent? The detective squad leader did not notify the judicial authorities immediately after the incident and did not take the necessary steps immediately, which was also a dereliction of duty. Ybarnégaray concluded that the parliament should do something today so as not to fail the trust of the people. Former Prime Minister Herriot, leader of the Radical Socialist Party, then proposed a motion in the name of the party, saying that he believed that the government would do its duty and at the same time demanded that the judiciary strictly enforce the law and not have any scruples. The Socialist Party also proposed a motion calling for the reform of the police and judiciary and to expose the truth about the swindle case. The Communist Party's motion advocated that a committee be jointly organized by the two houses of parliament to conduct an investigation. Parliamentarian Ybarnégaray also put forward a motion in the name of the right-wing central party, requesting that 44 members of the House of Representatives organize an investigation committee. Former Prime Minister Herriot strongly advocated the motion he proposed to trust the government, saying that over the years, banks had gone bankrupt, and the people had suffered great losses, but he had never heard of any investigations. Why would such a method be used this time? "He doesn't want to hide anything, and wants to investigate thoroughly." Herriot protested against some parties' use of the swindle case to attack left-wing figures. At 5:25 PM, the meeting was adjourned for a moment. The Socialist Party decided during the break to vote in favor of the motion proposed by Herriot, expressing confidence in the government, and opposing the appointment of an investigation committee. At this time, the government's ability to obtain the support of a majority has become a foregone conclusion. The meeting continued at 5:35 PM. Socialist parliamentarian Olivoor demanded that the House of Representatives quickly pass various laws to protect savings undertakings. He also said that he was not able to agree with Ybarnégaray's motion to appoint an investigation committee. Former Prime Minister Théodore, leader of the right-wing party, stood up to defend Ybarnégaray's proposal, saying that in the past, whenever financial malfeasance occurred, the Socialist Party advocated the organization of an investigation committee. Why did it not agree this time? Moreover, which country does not have financial malfeasance cases? Isn't France the only one? Since there is this case, it should be investigated jointly by all political parties instead of always entrusting this responsibility to the government. Subsequently, Prime Minister Chaudemps declared that the government had decided to reorganize the judiciary and the judicial police affairs, but the reorganization should be done calmly and peacefully and not hastily. He should investigate Ybarnégaray's criticism of the detective squad's negligence to clarify responsibility. However, if an investigation committee is organized, the procedures will be cumbersome and will probably delay the time, so that the truth cannot be revealed, and the current government can also shirk its responsibility, because most of the facts of the swindle case occurred long before he took office. At 9:50 PM, the meeting was temporarily suspended. Finally, the House of Representatives voted on the interpellation. In the end, it voted to trust the government by a vote of 360 to 229, rejecting the motion to organize a parliamentary investigation committee, and passed the motion proposed by Herriot by a vote of 378 to 205. (Havas, 12th)

French Revolutionary Conspiracy

A Five-Man Directorate Discovered by the Police

(Paris) Someone in Paris was conspiring to implement a five-man directorate when the government was overthrown due to the Bayonne swindle case. Fortunately, it was discovered by the police and prevented from being realized. It is reported that these people intended to follow the five-man directorate method implemented during the French First Republic from 1795 to 1799, and had already appointed five people as follows: former President Doumergue, Senator Caillaux, the famous general of the Great War Weygand, Paris Police Chief Chiappe, and Radical Socialist leader Daladier. However, according to the police investigation, none of the people who were nominated knew about it. (Guomin, 13th)

Herriot and Théodore Engaged in a Heated Verbal Sparring Match: One Calm, One Quite Indignant

Although today's meeting in the House of Representatives was not as intense as yesterday's in the debate on the swindle case, the two former prime ministers Herriot and Théodore engaged in a heated verbal sparring match. Herriot defended the Radical Party's motive for trusting the government, mentioning the country's aid to banks in difficult situations. Théodore refuted it, saying, "Are you saying that Stéeg (former Radical Party Prime Minister) lent 100 million francs to the Alsace-Lorraine Bank?" Herriot replied calmly and with a smile, "I am referring to the fact that you should send, not lend, 200 million francs to the National Credit Bank." A parliamentarian from Théodore's party stood up and claimed that the National Credit Bank had returned 170 million francs last year, but Finance Minister Bonnet immediately replied that as of today, the bank still owed a total of 200 million francs and hoped that 150 million francs could be recovered next year. Thereupon, Théodore, amid the emotional tension, threw up his sleeves and left the parliament. The atmosphere then returned to calmness. Herriot's speech then returned to the main topic. Before long, Théodore re-entered the parliament and denounced Lafont, a parliamentarian from the New Socialist Party, as a liar, which again caused an uproar. Finally, Théodore claimed that he supported the motion to organize a thorough investigation committee, that he opposed dictatorship in the Republican principle, and that he believed that there was absolutely no question of a coup. Paris was calm as usual at night. Indeed, many young people stood in the streets in the rain, but no incidents occurred and the police did not have to intervene. (Reuters, 12th)

German Communist Party Female Parliamentarian's Estate Confiscated

(Berlin) The mansion of Mrs. Zietkin, leader of the German Communist Party, on the outskirts of Berlin was ordered to be confiscated today by the Prussian State Government. Annual Meeting of the Land Administration Society to be Held in Zhenjiang Today

(Nanjing) The Land Administration Society is scheduled to convene its first general meeting in Zhenjiang starting from the 14th. Attendees include Wang Qiyun. The purpose of this meeting is to discuss methods for land consolidation in China. Land is where mankind resides and is the foundation for all material equipment. Human needs such as clothing, food, housing, and transportation, as well as all construction materials, originate from the land. Therefore, the formation and development of a region's systems and culture often depend on the proper use of land and the appropriate distribution of land rights. Land should be based on the principle of equality to address the drawbacks of private land ownership. More than eighty members and over twenty group members are expected to attend this conference. The Ministry of Interior, the General Staff Headquarters, the Land Survey Bureau, the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, the Civil Affairs Departments of various provinces, municipal governments, and land social bureaus are required to send representatives. The central government has designated Chen Guofu, and the Ministry of Education has designated Zhou Fo Hai to deliver instructions. The proposals to be discussed during the meeting include: (A) Issues concerning the procedures for land consolidation in China: (1) formal surveying and registration; (2) simplified consolidation; (B) The focus of land issues in China: (1) tenancy system; (2) land utilization. (Special dispatch from the 13th)

Kong Xiangxi's Chauffeur Opens Fire, Injuring a Police Officer on Duty; Case Sent to Court for Prosecution

The Current Situation in Northeast China Under Japanese Iron Heel

— Zheng Dong

(Correspondence from Changchun) (1)

Japan's invasion of Northeast China has always had a consistent plan. The sudden outbreak of the September 18th Incident was merely the realization of its continental policy. Looking back at the progress of the Japanese iron heel's advancement into Manchuria since September 18th, two years have passed. In this auspicious springtime of the third year, the Japanese warlords are loudly singing their songs of victory on our plains. Today, they are not only following their planned course, but also actively implementing their insidious annexation tactics. The current Governor-General of Korea, Ugaki Kazushige, once said, "From now on, we can use the experience of governing Korea to govern Manchuria, and with past experience, we will have even greater confidence in completing it quickly..." What should our countrymen think upon hearing this? Japan is playing puppet games, performing its two-man comedy, while implementing Japanese-Manchurian economic control, exploiting the blood and sweat of our compatriots in Northeast China, and driving our people in Northeast China to be cattle and horses, while they act as supreme emperors, reaping the benefits and doing whatever they want. All of this is probably unimaginable for our countrymen far away in the interior. Hereafter, I wish to record what I have seen and learned through inquiries and present it to our countrymen. Having endured countless dangers and interrogations to get here, and with no freedom to submit manuscripts, I must risk doing so out of conscience. I will elaborate as follows:

I. Ironclad Evidence of Japanese Rule in the Puppet State

Since seizing Northeast China, Japan has created the so-called "Manchukuo," establishing government offices and counties, creating a grand and imposing façade, seemingly forming a country. However, all important positions within the government are filled by Japanese. According to my investigation, from June of last year to the present, although the majority of administrative personnel in various organizations, large and small, are traitors, and each organization is headed by a traitor, the real power, such as department chiefs and section chiefs, is entirely held by Japanese. Japanese employees hold the real power, while the traitors are merely puppets living on stipends. This is ironclad evidence of Japanese manipulation of the puppet state, which no one can deny. Take the State Council as an example: among the more than 700 employees, more than 300 are Japanese, which speaks volumes. Below is a list of the names, positions, and comparisons of Japanese and puppet officials in the puppet state. Although the material may be dry, it is important data on the Japanese rule in the puppet state.

Hunan Remnant Bandits Divide and Flee

Chen Jicheng Plans to Encircle and Suppress the Eight-Doo Mountain Bandit Stronghold

Hunan Special Political Bureau Decides to Establish Daban City

Hankou Correspondence: Kong Hechong's remnant bandits, around mid-December of last year, launched a large-scale intrusion into Hunan, and the bandit flames flared up for a time. Counties such as Zhang, Puchi, Chongyang, and Tongshan successively reported alarms, and Xueguanfan, Yanglinfan, and Eight-Doo Mountain in the western border of Chongyang all fell into bandit strongholds. The Joint Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui received the report and immediately ordered He Chengjun to dispatch troops to provide assistance and send aircraft for reconnaissance and bombing. He Jian also telegraphed Chen Jicheng, commander of the Third Column, to supervise Feng Xingxian, Guo Runan, and Li Jue's departments, as well as the security teams of various counties, to encircle and suppress from all sides. By the 27th, the deployment of various armies was ready and operations began. After seven days of fierce fighting with the bandits, by January 2nd of this year, the bandit crowd was largely defeated, and the serious situation suddenly eased. After being hit hard, the bandits abandoned their plan to capture Chongyang and fled in four groups: one group fled to Hongshang, Hongxia, and Dongping on the border of Chong and Pu; one group fled to Heiqiao and Bankeng on the border of Chong and Xian; one group fled to Xiaosaping, Tangkou, Dadonggang, and Xiaodonggang on the border of Chong and Tong; and one group fled to Mushigang under the jurisdiction of Yangxin County. Xueguanfan, Yanglinfan, and Eight-Doo Mountain also remained in the hands of the bandits. On the 7th, Chen Jicheng transferred troops to Huzhaoshi in the west of Chongyang County, first advancing to Xueguanfan and Yanglinfan to suppress them, and at the same time sent teams to search the Hongshang, Hongxia, and Taohualing areas to protect Chongpu's transportation. After each route gained an advantage, he would unite with the garrison troops and teams in Linxiang, Tongcheng, and Puchi to launch a large-scale attack on the Eight-Doo Mountain bandit stronghold. Chen considered that Moushi in Yangxin County, which is adjacent to Tongshan and other counties, was an important town in southern Hunan. In order to advance both military and political affairs, he specially requested Chairman Chiang to establish a special political bureau there. Chairman Chiang had approved it, ordering the Hunan Provincial Government to send personnel for inspection and determine measures. The general bureau site would be located in the center of Daban City, with one bureau chief, to be selected by the Third Column Command and requested by the Provincial Government for appointment, and reported to the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters for record. The expenses would be paid by the Provincial Government according to the first-class example. It is heard that it may be organized and established at the end of this month or the beginning of next month. (12th)

Transportation on the Border of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Fujian

Highway Transportation Has Been Completed

Jiangxi-Zhejiang Railway Actively Under Construction

Nanchang Correspondence: On the border of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Fujian, there are the Yandang and Wuyi mountains standing between them, and transportation has always been rugged. Since the completion of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the Jiangxi-Zhejiang motor road has also been opened to traffic, connecting to Yushan. It only takes eight hours from Nanchang to Yushan, and no more than one day from Yushan to Hangzhou. During this anti-rebellion military campaign, the Jiangxi-Zhejiang and Hangzhou-Jiangshan railways became the hub of military transportation. However, from the junction of Jiangxi and Zhejiang into Fujian, the car is still not in line, and the horses cannot go side by side. Zhao Guantao first rushed to build the Guangfeng-Pucheng highway, which is connected to the Jiangxi-Zhejiang and Hangzhou-Jiangshan roads leading to Yushan. At the same time, Chairman Chiang appointed Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Construction Department, as the Director of the Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Fujian-Anhui Border Highway Office, and together with various departments, they separately built the Zhejiang-Fujian highway, from Jiangshan to Pucheng. The Jiangshan-Changshan-Guanhua-Quzhou-Lanxi to Shangrao-Yushan branch lines have also been connected. That is, from Pucheng to the counties near the border of the three provinces, it will also be accessible in all directions. According to people from Shangrao, Hekou is now the transportation center of eastern Jiangxi. From here, cars to Guangfeng and Pucheng are endless, but it is not economical to detour through Yushan. Guo, the Administrative Commissioner of Shangrao, has been ordered to build the Shangrao County to Forty-Eight Du Road on the Sanjiang Bridge section from Shangrao to Hekou, that is, to cross the lake at Hutantou into the Shang (Rao) Guang (Feng) section, and connect to Fujian to avoid detours. Also, regarding the conversion of the Jiangxi-Zhejiang motor road into a railway and connecting it to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan road, the authorities have been planning for a long time, and now it has become a reality. The funds and material purchases have been sorted out, and the Jiangxi and Zhejiang provinces and the Bank of China jointly plan to organize a railway company. The main purpose is to expand the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway into the Jiangxi-Zhejiang Railway, first building the Yushan-Nanchang section. In terms of technology, the Ministry of Railways plans to use 60-pound steel rails for combined transportation with Hangzhou-Jiangshan. In terms of funds, in addition to Jiangxi issuing 12 million public bonds, the Ministry of Railways will issue another 12 million public bonds for the company to raise funds. The company organization will set up a board of directors, with two representatives from the railway and the Jiangxi and Zhejiang provinces, and four from the banking sector. After all parties agree, the Ministry of Railways will submit it to the Executive Yuan for approval and implementation. (January 9)

Bandit Suppression and Road Construction in Southern Jiangxi

Remnant Bandits in Changhewei Lianhu Have Been Defeated

Xionggang Trunk Road Can Be Completed by the End of This Month

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Yu Hanmou, the commander of the First Guangdong Army, returned to defend southern Jiangxi, he has supervised and led his troops to clear up the remnant bandits, and has repeatedly captured them. According to Deng Qichang, the head of the Second Division's Training Regiment, reported on the 3rd, at the end of last month, more than 600 communist bandits from the pseudo-22nd Division's 64th Regiment attacked Changhewei near Anyuan. The 5th Regiment of the Second Division stationed in Chongshiwei immediately sent two battalions of soldiers to suppress them. They encountered the bandits at Anbei. The bandits stubbornly resisted based on the high mountains. After about three hours of fierce fighting, our Third Battalion launched a fierce attack on the bandit position. At about 4 pm, the bandits on the mountain were defeated. At 7 pm, the team returned to Chongshi. In this battle, more than ten bandits were killed, one platoon leader was captured alive, and dozens of bandit rifles and ten steel helmets were seized. At the beginning of this month, Yu Hanmou went to Xinfeng on patrol again. Suddenly, it was reported that more than 700 communist bandits suddenly appeared in Lianhu, north of Xinfeng, and attempted to harass various villages and towns. Yu immediately withdrew Chen Zhang's department, Liang Rongqiu's regiment, from the Second Independent Brigade to encircle them. Liang's regiment first lured the communist bandits closer, and then encircled them from three sides. After four hours of fierce fighting between the two sides, the bandits were unable to support themselves and fled to Mount Baimei. More than half of the bandits were killed or wounded. Recently, there have been no bandit traces near Lianhu.

Since the remnant bandits in more than ten counties in southern Jiangxi have been successively cleared, the aftermath is now being actively handled. The military authorities, on the one hand, ordered the counties to strengthen their walls and clear the fields to prevent the remnant bandits from stealing and launching attacks, and on the other hand, they are rushing to build roads to promote local interests and facilitate transportation. It is found that the first trunk line of the southern Jiangxi highway starts from Nanxiong on the Guangdong border, passes through Dayu in Jiangxi, and reaches Nankang, up to Ganzhou. The roadbed has been built, but the bridges in the Xincheng section between Dayu and Nankang have not yet been completed. The bridges and culverts in the section from Nankang to Ganzhou are also under construction. The entire road will be completed by the end of this month. If the Xionggang Road is successful, it can be connected to the Shaoxiong Road to the south. At that time, it will be possible to drive from Shaoguan in Guangdong to Ganzhou City, which is of great significance to the transportation between Jiangxi and Guangdong. In addition, the Sanan lines are also connected to various counties on the Guangdong border. The Qiannan line can be connected to Wengyuan in northern Guangdong, and the Longnan line can reach Lianping and Heping in northeastern Guangdong. The former has already been opened to traffic, and the latter is also under construction. The Sanan roads are connected to each other, opening up another line, exiting Wangmudu, and connecting to the Yu Kang trunk line. The road from Xinfeng to Nanxiong has been completed, and the section from Xinfeng to Ganzhou has also been more than half completed. To the west of Ganzhou, there is the Shangchong Highway, from Shangyou to Chongyi, and the Chongnan Highway, from Chongyi to Nankang. The road lines have completed eighty or ninety percent. The above-mentioned road projects have been built by the First Army Department using the military-industrial system, so the development has been rapid. Recently, the Southern Jiangxi Administrative Office was established, and the Southern Jiangxi Highway Office will be organized by the Transportation Construction Section of the office to manage highway transportation matters in various subordinate areas. (January 8)

Hebei Province Forms Provincial Security Office

Commands Police and Militia Throughout the Province

Tianjin Correspondence: The Hebei Provincial Government believes that due to the war in eastern Hebei last year, people's livelihoods were depleted, order has not been restored, and the counties in southern Hebei were again hit by the Yellow River flood, society is unstable, and the countryside is bankrupt, resulting in frequent bandit atmosphere in various places, especially in the eastern Hebei area, where bandits have never been completely suppressed. Due to the restrictions of the war zone agreement, heavy firearms and troops cannot be sent there. The bandits know the hidden information and harass them even more. Although the counties have militia organizations, they are mostly recruited. They have no connection with the stationed security team, and they are unwilling to obey the command of a county magistrate when something happens. Therefore, although the militia is set up, it is not very effective. Yu Xuezhong, in view of this before the New Year, organized the Hebei Provincial Security Office. Its purpose is to unify the command of the militia police in the province, eliminate past malpractices, and form a whole useful organization. If a military incident occurs, the Security Office can command it at any time. The police and militia in the counties will act in unison. All service personnel in the office are transferred from the Hebei Civil Affairs Department's Security Committee, Police Department, and Provincial Government Secretariat. It is scheduled to be formally established in the middle of this month and attached to the Provincial Government. The Civil Affairs Department also notified the counties to cancel the recruitment of defense groups in the counties from this month and change it to a conscription method. Each village household will conscript six or seven people, and fewer will conscript three or four people. The conscription age is limited from 20 to 40 years old. After conscription, they will be trained for three months, and after the expiration, they will return to their villages. If something happens, they will be summoned by the counties and towns by order. The purpose is to hide soldiers in the agriculture, without spending public funds, and implement the self-defense of the people. Today (September), the Provincial Government also discussed and passed the organizational outline of the Security Office. The articles are as follows: (Article 1) The Hebei Provincial Government is to command special police teams, security teams, and promote the efficiency of defense groups in the province, and set up the Hebei Provincial Security Office. (Article 2) The Security Office will have one director, concurrently held by the chairman of the Provincial Government, and two deputy directors, concurrently held by the director. (Article 3) The Security Office will have one inspector general, concurrently held by the head of the Police Department, three section chiefs, and six to nine section members, who will be dispatched by the director from the staff of the relevant agencies. (Article 4) The Security Office is divided into three sections, and its responsibilities are as follows: (1) General Affairs Section, in charge of documents, seals, personnel, law enforcement, communication, general affairs, etc. (2) Training Section, in charge of organization, dispatch, training, and intelligence, etc. (3) Management Section, in charge of salary, ammunition, uniforms, etc. (Article 5) Each section of the Security Office may handle matters in groups depending on the situation. (Article 6) All personnel of the Security Office, from section members and above, are unpaid. Clerks and below may be paid a salary. Each section may employ employees and clerks as needed. (Article 7) The Security Office uses presentations to the Provincial Government, orders to the counties and teams, and letters to other unrelated agencies. (Article 8) The expenses of the Security Office shall be budgeted by the Provincial Government and issued by the Finance Department. (Article 9) The official seal of the Security Office shall be issued by the Provincial Government. (Article 10) The detailed rules for the operation of each section of the Security Office shall be formulated separately. (Article 11) This outline shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Provincial Government. (9th)

Jiangsu Construction Director Talks About the Actual Situation of Conscripting Labor to Repair and Dredge the Liutang River

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Government actively prepared for the project of conscripting labor to repair and dredge the Liutang River, the counties along the river have recently started work one after another. The Current Affairs News Weekly Review on the 7th of this month raised four questions about this move. The reporter specially visited Director Shen of the Construction Department to inquire about his opinions. Director Shen explained them one by one as follows: "I have also seen the comments in the newspaper. I think it is because I have not been able to understand the actual situation, which led to these speculations. The first point, regarding the issue of wages, is not that the wage is 7.5 cents per person per day, but it is still priced by the square. The unit price is determined according to the experience of conscripting labor in various places and the current actual situation. The provincial government convened the county magistrates to come to the province to discuss and set the minimum price for building dikes at 4 cents per cubic meter, the highest at 6 cents, and the average at 5 cents. The minimum price for digging rivers is 7 cents per cubic meter, the maximum is 10 cents, and the average is 8.5 cents. On average, each person can build 3 to 4 cubic meters of dikes or dig about 2 cubic meters of rivers per day, then each person can earn more than 15 cents per day, which can maintain their livelihood. The stipulation of this square price takes into account the financial difficulties of the provincial government, striving to handle it by conscripting labor, and at the same time taking into account the difficulty of the workers' lives, and still pricing by the square. Therefore, after several consultations, it is considered very appropriate. The second point, regarding the issue of corruption, the provincial government has also paid attention to this for a long time. When the county magistrates' meeting was convened in October last year, Chairman Chen gave a thorough explanation and specially urged that if there is any fraud such as bullying the villagers and deducting from it to seek profit, the county magistrates should be severely punished at any time, and the county magistrates who are also the section chiefs of each section should also set an example and be a model for all staff members. Afterwards, we should still send personnel to conduct secret investigations at any time. The third point, regarding the issue of the quality of the workers, although there are tens of thousands of workers conscripted this time, they are all divided according to the number of acres, and most of them are peaceful farmers along the river, all of whom have permanent property. They have also been compiled into rows and teams, and the township and district chiefs are also the captains and team leaders to lead the work. It can be avoided to cause trouble by borrowing. Moreover, since this project has a direct stake, the local people are extremely clear. Even if bad elements mix in, not only should the government strictly eliminate them, but also the good workers will not tolerate them. The fourth point, regarding the issue of how to settle the workers after the completion of the work, the workers conscripted are farmers along the river, and they work using the agricultural gap period. After the work is completed, they return to farming, and there is no need to find another way. It is estimated that when the Liutang River project is completed, it will be the time when farming is about to begin, and the farmers can continue to engage in agriculture."

Songjiang

Catching Gambling, Gun Wounds Neighbor

Yesterday (12th), the patrol officer of the Fourth Branch reported that there was gambling in Gu Musheng's house in the 20th map of Baiwo Township Guang ○ An. He sent a squad leader to arrest him and arrested Gu Musheng, the head of the gambling, and six gamblers. At that time, the dog barked, and neighbor Gu Jinxiang opened the door to see what happened, and was shot in the left foot by the police's gun, and blood flowed like a column. His family carried him to Songjiang Hospital for treatment. The diagnosis was that he was shot by a pistol, the bullet pierced through, and the ankle bone was broken. The injured person was unwilling and reported to the county court for examination. It is heard that the patrol officer of the Fourth Branch detained two police officers who caused the accident and sent them to the head office for review. It is heard that Gu Musheng, the head of the gambling, was sentenced to 20 days of detention, and the rest were punished separately.

Suzhou

Lake Bandit "Little Overlord" Captured

The fugitive "Little Overlord" in the case of the lake bandit Geng Mazi, who has been executed, namely An Er, secretly returned to Taihu Lake and tried to start a gang, hiding in a duck shed by the Zhoujiadang Lake near Wujiang. Yesterday (13th) at dawn, He Linchun, the captain of the Wujiang County Water Patrol Team, personally led the detectives and captured him without a sound. According to the confession of the team leader after interrogation, he admitted that he had committed robberies, kidnappings and extortions with Liu Aizi Geng Mazi and others. He was immediately sent to the county for interrogation.

Jiading

Fourth District Chief Accused

Yang Xiafen, the district chief of the Fourth District Office of Waigang, was jointly reported by Lu Tiehua, the township chief of the district, and twelve others to the Civil Affairs Department and the county government, accusing him of encroaching on public funds such as the township office, the security regiment, and the Baoyuantang, not often coming to the office, neglecting district affairs, and being corrupt and derelict. The county government has ordered Huang Sun, the district chief of the First District, to investigate and reply.

Five Prisoners Died in Succession

The prison in the county government is very crowded, and the air is turbid. In December last year, two prisoners died in succession. On January 2nd of this year, a prisoner named Zhu Aidi died. On the 7th, a prisoner named Yan Zidi died. On the 8th, Liu Haishan died again. A total of five prisoners died in succession in eleven days. The disease was initial swelling of the feet, followed by swelling of the head and chest, leading to death. The conditions of the prisoners were the same.

Wuxi

Xiyi Road to Open Next Month

The Xiyi Highway has been actively underway since the Jiangnan Automobile Company submitted an application to the Construction Department to collect and repair the road surface. Now the section from Yixing to Heqiao has been completed and opened to traffic on the 5th of this month. The remaining road works from Heqiao to Wanshi Bridge, Huangyan Bridge, Panjia Bridge, ○○ Bridge, Yangwan, Mei ○, and Wuxi are now being actively built and will be completed in early February. At the same time, the entire road will be opened to traffic. The full-route passenger ticket price from Wuxi to Yixing is set at 2.2 yuan.

Qingsheng Theater Reopened

The Qingsheng Theater outside Guangfu Gate on Dongxin Road in this county was closed on the 11th because it refused to be inspected by the garrison. Now it is learned that the battalion was ordered to patrol because it was responsible for defending the place. The theater dared to resist and injure the patrol team soldiers, fearing that reactionary elements were lurking in it, so the theater was temporarily sealed off for investigation. Later, the manager of the theater found out that the tea boy Li Ronglin and Fan Rongsheng, who caused the incident, and sent them to the camp for handling. The camp learned the truth and transferred the murderers to the Public Security Bureau for punishment and reopened the theater. The theater resumed business as usual on the same day.

Zhenjiang

Wu Junyu Sent to Suzhou for Trial

Wu Junyu, the former director of the Kunshan County Construction Bureau, owed more than 27,000 yuan in public bonds during his four years in office. He was previously placed under custody by the provincial government and transferred to the Zhenjiang District Court for handling. After investigation, he was transferred to the Criminal Court for trial on the charge of embezzling public bonds. At the end of the debate, he was sentenced to two years and eight months of imprisonment, deprived of public rights for eight years, and ordered to repay 27,316 yuan, six jiao, and two li of construction public bonds in the attached private lawsuit. Wu declared in court that he would not accept the judgment and appealed to the Suzhou High Court. The High Court approved the appeal and ordered a trial in Suzhou. After receiving the order, the Zhenjiang Court ordered the bailiffs to send Wu to Suzhou for trial yesterday.

Chen Lu, the director of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, summoned Ni to the bureau. Therefore, the local Chamber of Commerce formally requested the Huainan Deputy Transport Envoy to handle it according to law for privately raising salt prices and disrupting the market, and reported it to the Public Security Bureau to maintain order.

The ten-mile-long street in Hebei outside the city is guarded by the Public Security Bureau; 3. The opening and closing of the city gates are scheduled at 6 am and 10 pm every day; 4. The area outside the city walls in the south, east, north, and west is patrolled by the security team; 5. Hotels, theaters, and incoming ships are inspected by the patrol team, and ports are inspected by the Public Security Bureau; 6. No troops of any kind are allowed to wander around for no reason. Once discovered, they will be sent to the regiment for investigation; 7. Soldiers are not allowed to watch plays unless it is Sunday afternoon; 8. The security team should also be neatly dressed and not go out unless it is for official business.

Association to Promote National Goods Requests Tax Increase on Japanese Light Bulbs

Hu Xiyuan Visited Tang Haian to Request Meeting

According to an investigation by the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods, Japanese merchants are practicing dumping due to overproduction. Various goods are being shipped to China in large quantities, which is severely affecting the entire national goods industry, especially the electrical appliance industry. The Shanghai Electrical Appliance Manufacturers Association and member factories of the light bulb industry have sent letters requesting relief to survive. The third joint meeting of the 14th Executive and Supervisory Committees decided to submit requests to both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to seek remedies. The original submission is recorded below:

Submitting that Japanese goods, electric light bulbs, are imported as raw materials to reduce taxes. We sincerely request that you instruct customs in various places to levy taxes on all goods as finished products to prevent taking advantage of loopholes and to protect national goods. The various members of the Shanghai Electrical Appliance Manufacturers Association and the member factories that manufacture electric light bulbs have sent letters stating that Japanese merchants have recently imported light bulbs without copper heads as raw materials to reduce taxes, resulting in lower costs and undercutting prices. This is implementing a dumping policy, which has greatly harmed the national light bulb factories. Goods are stagnant and sales are sluggish, leading to a standstill. All workers are facing the panic of unemployment. This matter concerns the future of the national goods industry and is of great importance. Please provide relief to maintain our survival, etc.

We have investigated that Japanese merchants are cunning by nature and practice dumping, which harms all national goods, especially the electrical appliance industry. They import light bulbs without copper heads as raw materials, deceiving customs to steal and reduce import tax rates, lowering costs, disrupting the market, and squeezing out national goods. Their intentions are vicious. If we do not find a countermeasure soon, the national light bulb factories will suffer serious damage and all will be shut down, creating social unrest. The association has an unshirkable responsibility to protect national goods. It is appropriate to submit a request to your ministry, requesting the Ministry of Finance) to instruct customs in various places to levy taxes on all light bulbs as finished products imported in the aforementioned manner to prevent taking advantage of loopholes and to protect national goods. We anxiously await your instructions.

Xin Sheng News Agency said that Japanese headless light bulbs are imported and taxed as raw materials. Cunning merchants are also cleverly creating various brands to disrupt the market for genuine national light bulbs. This matter has already aroused serious attention in society. The Municipal Electrical Appliance Manufacturers Association has already telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry. The chairman of the association, Hu Xiyuan, met with Minister Chen Gongbo in Shanghai the other day and requested that the headless light bulbs be taxed as finished light bulbs as soon as possible. Minister Chen agreed on the spot, saying that he would rush back to the ministry to handle it and that it would be recorded. Yesterday, at the request of the other businesses, Mr. Hu revisited Tang Haian, the superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, to discuss increasing the import tax rate on headless light bulbs. It is reported that the superintendent of customs has already requested the Tax Affairs Department to pay close attention.

Japanese Side Denies Japanese Soldiers Landing in Fujian

Ariyoshi Says Japanese Residents Have All Withdrawn

The Japanese Daily News says that after the Fujian military suffered setbacks, all units were concentrated in the provincial capital of Fuzhou to fight to the death. The Central Army is also approaching the outskirts of Fuzhou, making battles in the provincial capital almost inevitable. The Japanese side is thinking of taking the opportunity to cause trouble, using the excuse of protecting Japanese residents. Yesterday morning, the newspaper reported that Japanese marines had already landed in Fuzhou. Yesterday morning, the reporter from the Japanese Daily News specifically visited Japanese Ambassador Ariyoshi. Counselor Ariyoshi responded to questions, and the conversation is recorded below.

Japanese Soldiers Have Not Landed

Mr. Ariyoshi first stated that the Japanese military authorities, in order to protect the lives and property of Japanese residents given the imminent outbreak of war in Fuzhou, did send warships carrying marines to Fujian to prepare for any eventuality, but the report that they had already landed in Fuzhou for guard duty is not true. We have not received a telegram about it either. However, when the time is right, that is, when the war breaks out, the Ministry of the Navy will order the marines to land south of the Nantai Bridge in Fuzhou to protect Japanese residents.

Two Ships Enter Min River

Currently, there are two Japanese warships in Fuzhou: the Hamakaze destroyer, originally stationed in Magong Port, and the Tatekaze warship. The Tatekaze warship was originally stationed in Xiamen, but now that Xiamen has been recaptured by the Chinese Navy and the area is safe, it has been ordered to come from Xiamen. Both ships have arrived in Fuzhou and entered the Min River. The number of marines carried on the ships is approximately two battalions. Because the areas where Japanese residents live are adjacent to the Min River, they can land for guard duty in a few minutes in case of emergency.

Japanese Residents All Withdraw

As for the report that Ambassador Ariyoshi refused to allow Japanese residents to move, this is no longer an issue. According to a telegram from Fuzhou Consul Moriya, the approximately 10,000 Japanese residents in Fuzhou have now all withdrawn outside the city to designated safe areas, that is, the Qiancangshan area south of the bridge. Because there are few houses and many people, some are temporarily living near the Japanese Consulate, the Peiyuan Elementary School, and the South China Women's University. The lives of the residents should be safe, but there are still a small number of Taiwanese and their property in the city that are difficult to move. We are still asking the Chinese authorities to find ways to protect them. The reporter also asked whether it was reported that the central government had sent Foreign Minister Tang Yuren to Shanghai to negotiate the withdrawal of Japanese residents with the Japanese ambassador. It is said that they have not heard of this. As for Xiamen, it is now peaceful as usual, and Japanese residents who cannot retreat are also not a problem.

Consular Corps Urges Fujian to Withdraw Troops

Mr. Ariyoshi said at the end that war clouds are spreading over Fuzhou. In recent days, consuls from China, Britain, and the United States have been meeting at the Japanese Consulate on Qiancangshan with Japanese Consul Moriya to discuss ways to protect foreign residents. There are not many British and American residents in Fujian, and they have already moved to Cangshan, but there are still churches, hospitals, and schools that cannot avoid being affected by artillery fire. Therefore, the consular corps has proposed to persuade the 19th Route Army to withdraw its troops from Fuzhou to avoid sacrificing the people, but for the sake of caution, it is still being considered.

Four Ministries Order New Regulations on Anti-Piracy Escorts for Sea Vessels

Naval Police and Customs Vessels Jointly Responsible for Anti-Piracy

Shanghai sea vessels suffered pirate attacks repeatedly last year. After various shipping companies petitioned the central government to suppress them, the Ministry of Transportation invited the Ministries of Interior, Navy, and Finance, along with representatives from the Shanghai China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Shipping Association, to discuss anti-piracy plans. After many meetings, practical measures for suppressing piracy and providing escorts have been formulated, and they will be implemented jointly with the various shipping companies in Shanghai. Recently, there have been several more cases of pirate attacks on merchant ships due to unrest in the sea. Therefore, the anti-piracy escort law will be implemented ahead of schedule. Yesterday, various shipping companies received the anti-piracy implementation law ordered by the four ministries. The reporter has investigated and recorded it as follows:

Four Ministries Formulate Measures

The Ministries of Transportation, Navy, Finance, and Interior, and Shanghai shipping representatives such as Shen Jiyun, discussed preventing pirate attacks on ships after the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yushun ship encountered a pirate attack last year. At that time, representatives of the various ministries believed that anti-piracy on sea vessels required the simultaneous assistance of the various ministries in order to achieve mutual benefit. In addition to dispatching naval vessels to provide escorts, shipping companies also need to improve construction. The four ministries have held many meetings on this case, and it has now been revised. The Ministry of Transportation has issued Instruction No. 74 to Shanghai, ordering the various shipping companies in this port to strictly comply.

Coastal Military Police Cooperate in Defense

The four ministries decided on 16 measures for suppressing piracy and providing escorts. Article 1: These regulations apply to the escort of passenger and cargo ships sailing from Chinese ports in coastal or ocean voyages. Article 2: The Navy Department, the Coastal Defense Command, and the Fleet are responsible for suppressing piracy and providing escorts on the water. The Ministry of Interior directs the land and water police officers under the jurisdiction of the coastal provinces' police agencies to be responsible for handling land routes and nearby islands and report them at any time. Article 3: The Coastal Defense Command will dispatch ships to be stationed and patrol the sea areas where pirates appear and where ships have been attacked.

Salt Customs Responsible for Smuggling Suppression

If customs and salt customs vessels hear of pirate alarms or know of pirate traces, they must immediately report to naval warships or the Coastal Defense Fleet. If there is a temporary request, they should provide assistance. Article 4: Naval warships and marines should do their best to assist if the anti-piracy forces of the Coastal Defense Command or the land and water police are insufficient. Article 5: The naval vessels should be responsible for rescuing when they receive distress signals from ships via wireless. Nearby customs and salt customs vessels should also go to rescue within the possible range and notify merchant ships on the same route to provide assistance.

Sea Vessels Equipped with Self-Defense Weapons

Article 6: The water police are responsible for protecting ships that run aground or run aground. Ships with suspicious circumstances should be prohibited from approaching. Article 7: Seagoing merchant ships should be equipped with self-defense guns and cannons in accordance with the regulations of the National Government's inspection of self-defense weapons. Article 8: The captain supervises the crew to train in the use of guns and cannons at any time. Article 9: Before the ship departs, suspicious passengers may be inspected by the local military police.

Wireless Radio Should Be Isolated

Article 10: Passengers' luggage and heavy objects should be stored in the hold. Article 11: Each ship should be equipped with wireless radio. Article 12: Each sea vessel should report to the designated radio station every four hours. If a distress signal is received, all agencies should be notified. Article 13: The wireless radio should be located at the highest point on the ship and completely isolated from the passenger cabin. The construction of the four walls, doors, windows, and upper cover must be able to withstand bullets. A telephone should be installed in the room to connect to the bridge and the pilot's platform.

Bridge and Other Modifications

Article 14: The four walls of each ship's bridge must be able to withstand bullets. In addition to the front glass windows and doors, steel windows and doors that open and close automatically should be installed. The steam steering gear should be installed inside the engine room. If the steering gears have been installed on the deck, they should be protected with steel plates. Article 15: On seagoing ships, all doors and windows connecting the engine room, boiler, and bridge with the passenger cabin must be locked at all times. They may not be opened without the permission of the supervising crew. The coal bunker openings on the deck should also be closed.

Shanghai Shipping Companies Have Implemented

Article 16: These regulations will be implemented three months after the Executive Yuan announces them. The new anti-piracy regulations are of great importance to the navigation safety of all ships. In addition to the four ministries ordering the land and water military police to comply, the various shipping companies and sea vessels in Shanghai have complied with the established methods, improved the anti-piracy settings of the various ships, and applied for self-defense guns and cannons to train the crew to use them.

Fourth Shipment of American Wheat Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Chinese Flour Mills Purchase and Are Specially Granted Tax Exemption

Docked at Buoy and Began Unloading in the Afternoon

The fourth batch of American wheat purchased by our government from the United States with loans arrived in Shanghai yesterday. It was purchased by Chinese flour mills, and the Ministry of Finance specially granted tax exemption. Docked at the buoy, it began unloading in the afternoon. The details are recorded as follows:

Four Batches Imported

The matter of transporting American loan cotton and wheat is handled by the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. He Molin, who was sent to the United States to charter ships to load, has returned to Shanghai. A total of three batches of American wheat have arrived in Shanghai, totaling five ships. As for the fourth batch, it was divided into two ships, totaling 16,782 tons. Among them, 7,832 tons were loaded on the Iron Ladenton liner, which entered the Wusongkou at 10:25 yesterday morning. The wheat loaded has all been purchased by Chinese flour mills, so it is docked at the Huangpu River buoy for the factories to pick up.

Unloading in the Afternoon

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent workers to the buoy to arrange in advance. Starting at 2:00 PM, the various flour mills that purchased the wheat successively sent ships to dock with the liner to pick up the wheat. It is expected to be unloaded within a week. As for the fourth batch of 8,950 tons loaded on the Harley Denton liner, it is expected to arrive in Shanghai within days and will also be docked at the buoy. These American wheat shipments were properly negotiated by the Central Bank's American Loan Cotton and Wheat Office and the Ministry of Finance, and special tax exemption was granted. The unloaded liners will be loaded with our country's export goods by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and returned to the United States.
