Chairman Han of Shandong Province Will Invite Industry Leaders from Shanghai to Solicit Opinions, Seeking Industrial Development

Mining Merchants to Jointly Establish a Large Company, Director Zhang Honglie Will Come to Shanghai to Discuss Construction

Mr. Qian Chengxu responded to Chairman Han of the Shandong Provincial Government's invitation last year to discuss various issues related to the development of the province's industry in a private manner. The plans presented by Mr. Qian, except for the coal production control aspect, have been adopted by the Shandong Provincial Government and the Qingdao Municipal Government, and they have begun to work together. There are also issues such as the construction of cotton and wheat warehouses and the improvement of cotton seeds, which the provincial government also considers extremely important and is planning. Soon there will be a method announced. After Mr. Qian returned to Shanghai a few days ago, the reporter of Xin Sheng News Agency went to meet him and discussed the following:

Coal Industry Control

"During this trip (Qian himself said), as far as I can see, Shandong's politics are on track and moving towards the construction stage. There are two things I have requested. The first is the control of coal. I advocate adopting a policy of separating production and jointly selling. Merchants should form their own companies to increase coal prices and quality, while limiting production to eliminate competition and unify the national coal front. Regarding this point, because coal exports and the coal market have a tendency to affect the interests of all parties, the steps taken by the provincial and municipal governments are extremely cautious, and the discussion time is also the longest. Finally, the opinions of the two governments have become consistent. Representatives from all parties have joined Qingji coal merchants to the Boshan and Zichuan areas along the Jiaoji Railway to convene local mine owners to further discuss the organization, and there is a possibility of establishing a company. Because the government is urging them very strictly, Zhang Honglie, director of the Shandong Construction Department, has also stated to the business community that if there is no solution, the government will never stand by. Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie has even set a time limit. The business community must establish a company preparatory office before the old lunar year ends."

Cotton and Wheat Warehouses

"Secondly, it is to construct cotton and wheat warehouses. I advocate adopting the Canadian wheat bank trust organization, concentrating all agricultural products in the province, building large-scale warehouses in appropriate areas, and issuing circulating warehouse receipts to raise prices and adjust finances. The result is that all inactive items can be converted into cash and circulated in rural areas. Farmers can rely on the guarantee of the items to obtain economic activity. It is estimated that the amount of various agricultural products in Shandong Province that can be used as collateral for issuing warehouse receipts is at least 100 million yuan in face value. To use this to relieve the rural areas is equivalent to increasing 100 million yuan in circulating capital. This matter is related to the revitalization of the rural areas, and the issue is extremely important. The provincial government is still considering it carefully. I am also collecting various materials on this type of organization these days, hoping to draft a concrete plan in a short period of time to facilitate promotion."

Abundant Products

"I didn't spend much time in Qingdao and Jinan, so I didn't have time to consult on other issues, but according to my observations, Shandong is rich in products and has a superior location, which is suitable for outside investment. First, land and water transportation is convenient, and transportation is not difficult. Second, although the location is in the center of the north and south, it is not a military zone. Third, all products, such as coal, cotton, wheat, tobacco leaves, and peanuts, are necessary items for industrial manufacturing in terms of power and raw materials. Promoting and developing them can meet the needs of the entire country for decades. Other places, such as Weixian, have inexhaustible raw materials, especially suitable for cotton spinning and cigarette manufacturing. Fourth, Shandong has the most important commercial ports and financial institutions, and it does not feel poor in financial scheduling for establishing industries. This is only in terms of economy. As for politics, under the governance of Chairman Han Fuqu in the past two years, Shandong has used millions of yuan for construction projects every year, and there are surpluses in the treasury and savings among the people. The so-called rural bankruptcy may exist elsewhere, but in Shandong, there is no sign of bankruptcy."

Striving for Construction

"The Provincial Department of Construction is the central hub for promoting various construction projects. Director Zhang Honglie is a student who studied in the United States and is excited about various organizations. Before I left, I told him that the world's economic situation is changing rapidly. In this complex society, doing things cannot be done by one person or one country alone. Therefore, this spring, I will come to Shanghai on a regular basis to specifically interview industry leaders and discuss the basic plans for Shandong's various construction projects in the future. Chairman Han's aspiration to revitalize Shandong's industry is also extremely eager. Soon, he will send invitations to industry leaders in Shanghai to go to Shandong to take a special trip. In addition to visiting the mountains and rivers everywhere, he also intends to solicit everyone's opinions for reference."

They left a simple written statement, stating that Jin Xi was illegally arrested by your consulate in coordination with Japanese police. Now, based on the two points of naturalization as a Chinese national and the judicial agreement of the concession, the French consulate should be responsible for his return. Also, before the negotiation of this case is resolved, the French consulate should seriously stop the transfer to Japan. This is of utmost importance. The original text of the joint submission of the various legal groups to the municipal government is recorded below. It is a submission regarding the illegal arrest of Jin Xi, requesting a serious protest to the French and Japanese consulates. It is submitted that Jin Xi, a national of the Republic of China, was illegally arrested by the French Central Patrol Room in coordination with the Japanese consulate on November 22, 1933. After repeated negotiations, he has not been released. Jin Xi is a national of the Republic of China. According to the exercise of the highest sovereignty of the country, no interference from any country is allowed. This time, the Japanese consulate arbitrarily arrested him, and the French consulate, without asking about the facts, hastily assisted, which is obviously an infringement of our country's sovereignty. Moreover, after the arrest, he was not transferred to the Chinese court for interrogation, but was directly handed over, which violated the concession agreement and endangered the safety of residents. If serious negotiations are not continued, not only will the country's prestige be swept away, but it will also create a bad precedent for future negotiations on naturalization. The submitters are all residents of Shanghai and are particularly concerned about the interests and harms of this issue. The public is indignant and difficult to remain silent. In addition to preparing to organize the Jin Case Support Association to thoroughly protest, we dare to ask the government to verify and quickly make a serious protest to the French and Japanese consulates to maintain sovereignty, which is in the public interest. Sincerely submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Six Point Plan for Subscribing to American Wheat and Flour

Submitted to the Ministry of Finance for Approval Yesterday

Resolution Expected Upon Approval of Tax Exemption

Since the Ministry of Finance announced the new tariff rates on imported rice and wheat, the flour manufacturers of this city have repeatedly joined forces with manufacturers from various regions, sending representatives to petition the government authorities, requesting exemption from taxes on imported wheat and flour purchased before the announcement. Although the authorities have not yet readily agreed, the manufacturers believe that the amount of wheat and flour purchased this time is substantial. If they do not persistently request a reduction in tariffs, their losses will be unbearable. Therefore, they have repeatedly negotiated with the Ministry of Finance, and progress is gradually being made. A New News Agency reporter learned from relevant sources yesterday morning that the Ministry of Finance has proposed a compromise to the manufacturers, namely, that the manufacturers must subscribe to 240,000 tons of American wheat and 6.4 million bags of American flour (worth approximately US$4 million). The manufacturers have already agreed and submitted a plan for taking delivery to the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Finance yesterday morning, requesting approval. The plan mainly consists of the following points: (1) 240,000 tons of American wheat will arrive in China in five months, and the price will be settled in three installments, based on Chinese and foreign market conditions; (2) The composition of the American wheat will be 30% hard winter wheat and 70% No. 2 American white wheat; (3) 6.4 million bags of American flour will arrive in China in twelve months; (4) Except for the "Ren Ma," "Fu Shou," "Golden Money," and "Red Sun Dang Tian" brands, the quality of other brands of flour must be the same as the above four brands; (5) Import duties will be calculated based on a 5% reduction; (6) The government is requested to implement a refund of wheat tax for goods transported overseas and to the three northeastern provinces. If the above plan is approved by the Ministry of Finance, the manufacturers will be able to purchase the goods, and the request for tax exemption can also be resolved accordingly.

Ministry of Railways Standardizes Calculation Method for Joint Transportation Freight Rates

Calculating Surcharges and Liability Fees

Should be Based on a Percentage of the Freight Rate

Regarding the standardization of the calculation method for joint transportation freight rates, the Ministry of Railways issued a special instruction to the two Railway Administrations yesterday, stating: "The joint transportation of state-owned goods was resumed in November of last year. All methods for calculating freight rates must have unified regulations to benefit merchants and ensure fairness. Since the implementation of liability-based joint transportation by the Tianjin-Pukou, Shanghai-Nanjing, and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways in September of the 21st year, all liability, priority, and highest priority fees and surcharges have been calculated as a percentage of the unit freight rate for ordinary goods, in accordance with Article 40 of the General Rules for Liability Transportation. The total amount is then multiplied by the weight to arrive at the total freight. Therefore, the original price lists for liability-based joint transportation of goods on the three railways listed ordinary freight rates, surcharges, and liability fees separately, calculated on a unit basis. When domestic joint transportation was resumed in November of last year, the Ministry, due to time constraints,

Compilation of Freight Rates

was unable to compile the rates in time and instructed each railway to exchange freight rate tables for use, while also filling out and submitting forms to the Ministry in accordance with the format of the joint transportation price list promulgated by the Ministry, in order to compile them. The Ministry also issued Instruction No. 7323, announcing the method for calculating joint transportation freight rates for compliance. Currently, most of the freight rate tables filled out by each railway have been received, and the Ministry is rushing to compile a compilation of joint transportation freight rate tables for each railway. However, previously, the Tianjin-Pukou, Shanghai-Nanjing, and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways calculated surcharges and liability fees as a percentage of the price, while the temporary measures stipulated in Instruction No. 7323 calculate them as a percentage of the freight rate. Furthermore, some freight bills from each railway calculate them as a percentage of the price, while others calculate them as a percentage of the freight rate. Since the methods are not uniform, freight rates vary, which is not fair. After careful research, it has been determined that it is more convenient in terms of procedure and fairer in theory to calculate all surcharges and liability fees as a percentage of the freight rate. Hereafter,

Each Railway's Calculation

of surcharges and liability fees should be based on a percentage of the freight rate. That is, when calculating the freight for joint transportation of goods, the freight rate per 50 kilograms or per metric ton listed in the compilation should be multiplied by the weight of each batch of goods to be transported to obtain the total freight for each batch of goods. This total amount will be used as the standard for calculating surcharges and liability fees. The above method for calculating freight rates is not only simpler for the clerks of each railway to calculate, but the compilation of joint transportation freight rates can also only list the freight rate, without the need to calculate and list other surcharges and liability fees separately. The length will be reduced compared to before, the printing costs will be reduced compared to before, and it will be more convenient to use. Therefore, the compilation of joint transportation freight rate tables compiled by the Ministry this time will only list the freight rate and not other surcharges and liability fees. Once the compilation and printing are completed, it will be distributed for use immediately. The freight

Rounding of Mills

method will still be handled in accordance with the provisions of Item 1 of the method for calculating joint transportation freight rates resolved at the 16th Joint Transportation Conference. That is, the ordinary freight should be calculated to the nearest fen (cent), and the li (mill) should be rounded using the four-舍-五入 (round half up) method to determine the entry or exit (e.g., 4 li and 9 hao (tenth of a mill) are discarded, while 5 li are advanced to 1 fen). However, the amount of liability, priority, highest priority, and additional fees calculated based on the freight rate is extremely small, with only mills and less than one fen, and should all be collected as one fen. Regarding this point, Tianjin-Pukou and Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo are inconsistent. Tianjin-Pukou adopts the rounding method, while Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo adopts the four-舍-五入 method, which is different and unreasonable. Hereafter, when there is an extremely small amount of less than one fen, it should all be calculated as one fen. The total amount of joint transportation freight, if there are odd amounts of less than five fen, should be calculated as five fen, and if there are odd amounts of less than one jiao (dime), it should be calculated as one jiao. However, if there are odd amounts in the amount obtained by each railway, it should still be calculated as the odd amount. If there is an excess count, it should all belong to the railway of origin. Furthermore, liability-based joint transportation,

Decreasing Calculation

method has been stipulated by ministerial order and examples have been published on record. However, for the sake of convenient calculation and in line with the spirit of the above calculation methods, all surcharges and liability fees should be calculated as a percentage of the freight rate after progressive distance reduction. That is, the freight rate after progressive distance reduction should be used as the standard, and surcharges and liability fees should be added separately. The above calculation methods are listed and exemplified in the order, and copies are sent along with the order. It is hereby ordered to forward them to the relevant departments and joint transportation stations for compliance and standardization. This order has been issued to the Traffic and Accounting Departments for compliance."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables Request to Rectify Forcing Stores to Issue Invoices and Affix Stamps

Painstakingly Argues the Illegality of the Tax Bureau's Distorted Interpretation

Clarifies that Regulations Have No Power to Interfere

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "On the 12th of this month, according to a letter from the Beijing General Chamber of Commerce, the Hebei Provincial Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau and the Beijing Branch Bureau have repeatedly sent letters requesting notification to all stores that those selling goods worth one yuan or more must issue a sales invoice and affix a stamp accordingly. This Chamber believes that stamps are used as proof on deeds to protect rights and interests. If the parties voluntarily waive their right to have their rights guaranteed by proof, they cannot be forced to issue invoices, and since they cannot be forced to issue invoices, they cannot be forced to affix stamps. Now, the Bureau, in order to promote sales, does not hesitate to violate legal principles and forces all businesses to issue sales invoices when selling goods, which is unreasonable. May we ask if the purchaser is in a hurry to board a ship, or has a need to not wait long, or does not need the proof (for self-purchase and self-use), they must wait quietly for the invoice to be issued. This kind of behavior is truly obstructive. On December 30th of the 22nd year, this Chamber held an Executive Committee meeting, and at the same time, chairmen and representatives of various trade associations attended and stated their opinions, and resolved to send a letter to your Association to jointly submit a request to the Ministry of Finance for interpretation, so that it can be followed. We specially request that you examine and handle this matter and reply to us to show your public spirit." The utility of an invoice is that the purchaser is entrusted by others to make purchases on their behalf for credibility, or that the purchaser does not come to the store in person and the store orders someone to send it to them, so an invoice is issued for verification. If the person goes to the store to buy it themselves, the payment is made immediately, and the purchaser does not need the invoice for proof, and the store does not need to issue it. For example, if friends borrow money from each other, or because of mutual trust, they do not write a loan agreement, and the state legislature cannot force them to write an agreement or affix a stamp. The provisions of the Stamp Tax Regulations can only restrict what kind of proof must be affixed with a stamp, but cannot restrict the people from using written proof and not oral contracts. The regulations do not have this power to interfere, and the tax bureau cannot make extra-legal interpretations. It is reasonable to telegraph your Ministry for review and approval, and we humbly request that you make corrections for the public convenience. Respectfully, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

Shen Lianfang and Others Presided, Wang Yiting Officiated, Chu Minyi and Others Reported on Their Deeds, Many Guests Attended

More than 500 people attended, including Yu Youren and Chu Minyi. The details are as follows:

Order of the Assembly

(1) Opening of the meeting, all stand at attention, (2) sing the Party song, (3) pay the highest respect to the Party and National flags and the portrait of the President, (4) Chairman respectfully reads the President's will, (5) Chairman's speech, (6) perform the memorial ceremony: A. Sun Ke's Eulogy

The text of the eulogy by Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, reads: "In November of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, Mr. Zhou Xiangling of Huzhou passed away from illness in his hometown. The gentleman was well-versed in classical books and gained fame early in life. He held a heart of universal love and possessed the virtue of loyalty. He exhausted his efforts in local affairs for decades as if it was just one day. He weighed matters and deliberated on reason, and the people of both Zhejiang provinces were all benefited by his grace. Tracing his deeds, such as managing salt affairs, establishing factories, establishing schools, supplementing and transcribing the Siku Quanshu (Complete Library of the Four Treasuries) of the Zhejiang Wenlan Pavilion, and writing and engraving more than 30 kinds of books, it is difficult to describe them all in detail. His hometown respected his fine reputation, and the literati admired his morality. Suddenly, he transformed, and his voice spread throughout the world. Therefore, I write this eulogy: 'The mountains and rivers of Huzhou are beautiful and nurturing, giving birth to great and lush talents. Holding jade and grasping jade, his virtues are pure and his learning is rich. He promoted industry and commerce, and was a leader in industry and commerce. National economy and people's livelihood all relied on him for remedy. He paid attention to culture and spread his name throughout the universe. His talent and virtue were both complete, and his brilliance and substance were equal. Suddenly, he rode a crane, and heaven did not bless him. His character is admirable, and his name is long-lasting.'"

Assembly Sacrificial Text

(1) On the 13th day of January in the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the Huzhou Association of Shanghai, Huzhou Society, Zhejiang Huzhou Crepe Industry Association, the North Shanghai Middle School, the Huzhou Shanghai Small and Middle Schools, and the Nanxun Association, etc., respectfully offer clear wine and ordinary delicacies to the spirit of Mr. Xiangling, saying: "Alas, Heaven does not leave behind, and we have suddenly lost an elder statesman. The Star Rider's departure has shocked far and near. We respect the gentleman's bright and unique talent, born in Mingxi, and his family has inherited virtue. At a young age, he repeatedly gained fame. In the autumn wind, he forged his wings and dismissed his merits and fame. He ate a bowl of vegetable gruel and drank five dou of Pengze wine, holding a heart of indifference and maintaining a lofty self-respect. At a time when the world was in trouble, the government was reformed, and the governor summoned him. He refused the wheel of Pu and devoted himself to managing salt and affairs. The people of both Zhejiang provinces all pushed him as a giant. Taking advantage of his remaining courage, he reorganized the salt system, compiled the salt law, and planned in detail. The sea ban was opened and the rights and interests overflowed overseas. He manipulated finance, and he was the first to advocate for a commercial bank, naming it Xingye and starting in Asia. In the commercial war, he competed and improved the silk industry, invented manufacturing, and factories stood in forests. The gentleman's character can be a rule for the ancients, being humble in dealing with people and righteous in his heart.

The Shanghai-Hangzhou traffic is convenient, arriving in the evening after departing in the morning. Business and academic circles linked arms and arrived. He created the hometown association, and guests felt at home. He donated money to establish schools, and the buildings were majestic. He benefited his hometown, nurtured people and supported honesty, relieved poverty and benefited the people. It is difficult to describe with books. He preserved the essence of the nation and visited different books. He made up the missing books in Wenlan, and the storehouses were filled with precious books. He had many writings and did not enjoy being an official. He roamed through mountains and rivers and enjoyed famous sites. He paid tribute to the ancients from afar, discovered hidden secrets, and the breeze passed. People were gone, and tears flowed horizontally and vertically. The phoenix flew on the high hill, with disheveled hair in the wilderness. Facing the wind, he paid his respects with lychee, cinnabar, and plantain. The clouds of Song are dim, and the water is rippling. He speaks a thread of words, and the pain is clear, summoning the soul. Hopefully it will resonate." (2) On the 13th day of January in the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the Huzhou Association of Shanghai, Huzhou Society, Zhejiang Huzhou Crepe Industry Association, the North Shanghai Middle School, the Huzhou Shanghai Small and Middle Schools, and the Nanxun Association, etc., respectfully offer clear wine and ordinary delicacies to the spirit of Zhou Bainian, saying: "Oh, Heaven blesses the Han people, the room is moved, and the revolutionaries are the first to realize the wind and electricity. The gentleman, with his handsome appearance, rose up and followed. He adhered to the doctrine, and the Southern Society opened wide. He united his comrades, lifted left and right. The Republic was rebuilt, and he raised our national flag. The gentleman held a pure character and also possessed heroic posture. He worked hard in his early years, and his learning was secretly probed. He was beautiful and elegant, and was good at talent. He joined the righteous army in the Northern Expedition and participated in military opportunities. He participated in secrets and connected with Zou Mei. He called and ran, walking on danger as if on flat ground. His spirit was courageous, and who could violate it? He mended the sky and refined stones, and did not give up after a hundred setbacks. The gentleman's talent and learning are both practical and universal. He declared diligence in the Party and the country, and his reputation was brilliant. When he entered the supervision, his style was rare in the world. He rectified discipline and swept away the vines. He eliminated the five turbidities, and his loyalty was an example. But Heaven did not bless him, and lost this ring. The country was not yet settled, and the nan wood was suddenly destroyed. The snow monkey wept, and the frost goose cried. I am from the same village as the gentleman, and my friendship is not private. I look up to the mountains and admire them, and my spirit relies on the water. I return to the South Forest and walk around with ropes. I use the red flag to summon him, and may his soul return."

Lofty Ambition of the National Crisis Propaganda Group: A 30,000-Li Expedition to Commence on the 20th of This Month from Shanghai, Lasting Two Years and Covering More Than Thirty Ports

The Shanghai National Crisis Propaganda Group, organized by Shen Yiqian and other students from the Shanghai Fine Arts School, embarked on a national crisis propaganda campaign in the Yangtze River, North China, and Mongolian border areas in February of last year. They endured numerous hardships and worked extremely hard. The group has now received financial assistance from the central government and Mayor Wu of this city and is scheduled to embark on another expedition on the 20th of this month, lasting two years, covering more than thirty ports, and traveling 30,000 li, truly a lofty undertaking.

Purpose of This Trip

According to the group leader, Mr. Shen Yiqian, the purpose of this trip is threefold: First, to carry out national crisis propaganda, such as holding national crisis art exhibitions, anti-Japanese war exhibitions, and national goods exhibitions, as well as screening lantern slides and distributing books and pamphlets. They will also provide local news outlets with texts and photographs for public dissemination to spread the seeds of patriotism. Second, to gather information on the actual conditions, such as the lives of various ethnic groups, industry and commerce, products, transportation, climate, etc., using text, drawings, photography, and other methods, to collect and compile them into books for various sectors to reference, in order to break down the barriers between north and south. Third, to promote national goods, collect local products, hold public exhibitions, and promote the goal of saving the country through production.

Seven Members of the Group

The members of the group embarking on this expedition are Shen Yiqian, Yu Chuangshuo, Zhang Yi, Wang Bin, Huang Zhaochang, Gu Tingpeng, and Mo Pu, a total of seven people, led by group leader Shen Yiqian. Mr. Shen is from Jiangsu Province and previously studied at a Japanese school in this city. He knew many Japanese friends in his daily life. His admission to the Shanghai Fine Arts School was also through Japanese introduction. However, since the September 18th Incident, Mr. Shen considered the national hatred irreconcilable and severed ties with all his Japanese acquaintances. The teachers and students of the Shanghai Fine Arts School all praised him. His resolute organization of the National Crisis Propaganda Group to engage in practical work is truly commendable.

Ministry of Railways Allocates Four Locomotives to Expedite Joint Transportation of Goods

The Railway Bureau Slightly Repairs and Reorganizes Them

They Have Been Separately Put into Use Successively

In November of last year, a large quantity of goods for joint transportation across the river accumulated on the Jinpu Railway. The Ministry of Railways convened representatives from the Jinpu and Jinghu Railways to discuss ways to expedite the flow. It was decided that one train of through-transportation freight cars would run daily in both directions from Dakou, Tengxian, and Xuzhou to Shanghai, and from Linhuai Guan and Bengbu to Shanghai, Wuxi, or Changzhou. The Jinpu Railway would provide three locomotives and the Jinghu Railway would provide three to four trains of freight cars. Subsequently, the Ministry of Railways, considering that the locomotives of both railways were indeed insufficient, specially approved the allocation of four locomotives owned by the ministry for the exclusive use of these through-transportation freight cars. The locomotive department of this bureau has successively dispatched personnel to receive them. After the car workshop made slight repairs and reorganizations, they have been put into use separately.

Verdict Announced Yesterday in the Case of Embezzlement by Customs Clerks

Su Kunnian Sentenced to Five Years Imprisonment

Wang Yueren and Seven Others Sentenced to Two Years

Chen Guoliang Sentenced to Six Months

Private Lawsuit Portion to be Investigated and Handled

The sensational Jianghai Customs duty embezzlement case, involving the defendants Su Kunnian, Wang Yueren, Jiang Zhenhan, Chen Zhongshan, Shi Cunqiao, Wei Anxiang, Zhang Songtao, Sun Guozhang, and Chen Guoliang, has been thoroughly investigated and concluded by the criminal court of the local court, awaiting sentencing. Yesterday at 3 p.m., Judge Qian ordered the nine defendants, including Su Kunnian, to be brought to the court for questioning. The court announced that Su Kunnian was found guilty of forging 61 customs duty receipts and seals, violating Articles 225 and 234, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, and assisting in embezzlement in business, violating Article 44, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Code and Article 357, Paragraph 1 of the same law, and sentenced him to five years of imprisonment. Wang Yueren, Jiang Zhenhan, Chen Zhongshan, Shi Cunqiao, Wei Anxiang, Zhang Songtao, and Sun Guozhang were found guilty of stealing customs paper, violating Article 337, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, and engaging in embezzlement in business, acting as direct and important accomplices, and sentenced to two years of imprisonment each, in accordance with Article 44, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Code and Articles 225 and 357, Paragraph 1 of the same law. Chen Guoliang was found guilty of inciting the use of forged official documents and sentenced to six months of imprisonment. After the sentences were announced, the defendants were returned to custody to await the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison. The portion of the lawsuit related to the private claims of the Customs will be investigated and handled later.

Verdict in the Tang Jiapeng Assassination Case

Zhao Guangfu Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Tang Jiapeng, also known as A Yu, a Ningbo native and former manager of the Rongji amusement park in the Great World, was assassinated in front of the Great World at 1:30 a.m. on June 18th of last year. A stray bullet also killed Wu Guangcai, a pedestrian from Yangzhou. The case was investigated by the special agency of the French Concession police, supervised by Chief Kim Ku-lin, and detectives arrested the culprits Zhang Xiaosizi, also known as Zhang Tinggui, from Funing, and Zhao Guangfu from Yangzhou. They also confiscated the handgun used by Zhao to commit the murder. They were handed over to the Second Special District Court for public prosecution on charges of premeditated murder. The details of the interrogation have been previously reported. The trial has now concluded. Yesterday morning, trial judge Wu Fangjun presided over the case in the First Criminal Court and ordered the two defendants to be brought to the court. Zhao Guangfu was sentenced to life imprisonment for conspiracy to commit murder and deprived of his civil rights for life. Zhang Xiaosizi was sentenced to twenty years of imprisonment for assisting in the conspiracy to commit murder and deprived of his civil rights for life. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is finalized will be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. After the sentences were pronounced, the defendants were transferred to the detention center to await the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison.

Murder Suspects From Yancheng Arrested in Shanghai

Ling Youxin and His Son Are Major Suspects

Both Firmly Deny After Arrest

Fu Ruixiang, a 21-year-old man from Yancheng, Jiangbei, was severely beaten by five or six fellow villagers in Lijiazhuang, his hometown, on October 18th of last year for demanding repayment of a debt, resulting in Fu's death from serious injuries. Fu Ruixiang's father, Fu Yansheng, reported the incident to the Yancheng County government for examination and filed a complaint accusing the murderers Ling Jicheng, Ling Mazi, and others. The county government ordered a strict search, but the Lings had already fled upon hearing the news. Only Ling Jicheng's wife, Ling Jishi, was arrested, interrogated several times, and detained. After investigation, Fu learned that Ling Jishi's husband's brother Ling Youxin and Ling Yafeng, father and son, were involved in the case and had fled to No. 3937 Daxu Lane, Robert Road, in the Shanghai Public Concession. He came to Shanghai alone and secretly confirmed the information. He hired lawyer Pan Fengtang to file a complaint with the First Special District Court, requesting an investigation. The court approved the request and issued an arrest warrant, which was delivered to the Putuo Road Police Station. Detective Xu Huanxiao and Bao Tan Zhang Changkun, along with Fu Yansheng, secretly went to Daxu Lane at 5 p.m. the day before yesterday and arrested Ling Youxin (a 60-year-old man from Jiangbei) and Ling Yafeng (a 37-year-old man from Jiangbei), father and son, and took them to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Jiang Baolian presented the details of the case, requesting that the Lings be detained pending notification of the Yancheng County government to bring them back. Fu Yansheng stated that his son, Fu Ruixiang, was murdered by five or six people in Lijiazhuang, Yancheng. The prosecutor examined the body, and he filed a complaint with the county government. Later, he learned that Ling Youxin and his son were involved and had fled to Shanghai, so he tracked them to Shanghai and arrested them. He submitted the indictment and requested that the Lings be detained so that he could report back to the county government. When questioned, the Ling father and son denied assisting in the murder of Fu Ruixiang and jointly hired lawyer Jiang Yiping, stating that Ling Yafeng had brought his wife and children to Shanghai in January of the lunar calendar and was working as a laborer in the Zhaofeng Garden managed by the Public Works Department, earning 6 jiao per day, and was still working there without taking leave, so how could he have committed a crime in Jiangbei? This is truly unjust and the police should be ordered to investigate this point. His father, Ling Youxin, had been teaching in his hometown. In August of this year, he came to Shanghai after hearing the news that Yafeng's wife had died in Shanghai and had not returned. Furthermore, Fu Yansheng's complaint did not mention the names of the Ling father and son, so they were being falsely accused. Judge Wu Tingqi ordered the case to be postponed pending the arrival of documents from the Yancheng County government for further verification. The Lings were detained due to the seriousness of the case.

Rice Boat Owner Suddenly Assassinated

Shot While Walking With His Wife

The Reason for the Murder Remains Unknown

At around 9:30 last night, Jia Longgen, a 34-year-old man from Tangqiao Town, Pudong, who lived at No. 5 Kaitai Lane, Fengji Wharf, Nanshi, and worked in the rice boat business, was assassinated. He only had an elderly mother at home. Because of poverty, he became an adopted son-in-law to Shen Desheng, who operated a rice boat, and changed his name to Shen Adong. Therefore, he was known as Adong in the rice market. He was known as Jia Longgen. His wife, Amei, is 25 years old this year and is quite beautiful and fond of dressing up. Therefore, the couple lived in harmony. They owned two rice boats and personally operated them, transporting rice between Songjiang and Shanghai. Recently, two months ago, Jia Longgen fell ill, so they hired another boatman, and the couple moved ashore to the upstairs of No. 5. Amei also worked as a shaman (commonly known as a fortune teller), so she sometimes treated others for illness, which made their life slightly easier. Yesterday afternoon, around 8 o'clock, Li Xinzhi, a friend of Longgen who lived near the Wanchun Sauce Garden in Xuejia Bang, hired Amei to treat him because he was ill. The couple went out together. When they returned home, it was about 9:30. When Amei suddenly remembered that the patient still needed to send ghost horse papers, she turned around to go. Unexpectedly, at that time, a gunshot was suddenly heard from behind, and Longgen, who was walking with her, fell to the ground. Amei was flustered and only cared about her husband, forgetting about the murderer, so the thug escaped. Afterwards, the patrol police arrived after hearing the sound, but the murderer was gone. Only the body was lying on the side of the road, and his wife was crying beside him. They reported to the First District and First Precinct and inspected the scene. Amei was taken to the precinct for questioning. Today, at around 4 p.m., the court examined the body and found that he was assassinated by a thug. The bullet entered from the back of the head and exited from the eyebrow. The head was facing east and the feet were facing west. He was wearing a blue wool coat, a khaki flannel robe, felt shoes, and a duckbill cap. After the examination, the family prepared a coffin to collect the body. However, the underlying cause remains unknown. It is only hoped that the authorities will conduct a strict investigation so that the truth can be revealed.

Suzhou Creek Blocked Again

Boats Traverse the Water Surface

Visible for One or Two Li From a Distance

Suzhou Creek in this city is a transportation hub for inland rivers. The small ferries traveling to and from various places in Jiangsu and Zhejiang pass through the creek. The food, vegetables, and goods supplied to the residents of the city are also transported to Shanghai via this waterway. It is an important channel for inland water transportation. Last Saturday, it was blocked due to low tide and many boats. The water police station managed to clear it and allow passage. Unexpectedly, it was blocked again yesterday, and the number of boats blocked was even greater than before. The details are recorded as follows:

The Waterway Was Blocked on Tuesday and Wednesday. After the water police station managed to clear the blocked area, a large number of cargo ships arrived in Shanghai one after another on Friday night. When they reached the western section of Suzhou Creek in front of the Yangzhu Factory, the departing ships also arrived one after another. Due to the extremely cold weather and low tide, the arriving and departing boats were blocked again from that point. It was reported that several cargo ships were stranded in the river and could not move, causing more and more people to gather on both sides. The eastern section, starting from the Tianhou Palace Bridge, was completely blocked all the way to the front of the Yangzhu Factory.

Boats Stopped. Looking from the Old Garbage Bridge towards both sides, the river was full of boats, and the water surface was barely visible. The sounds of boatmen squeezing, jostling, and arguing filled the air. In the blocked section of the river, the boats traversed the water surface, and pedestrians could walk across the boats in the river without wading. From west to east, the small ferries, boats, barges, sailing boats, and other vessels of various sizes blocked totaled one or two thousand, stretching for one or two li.

Water Police Clearing. Yesterday, the water police station dispatched patrol boats and police officers to Suzhou Creek to clear the blocked waterway and restore traffic. However, it was impossible to move those stranded in the middle section. From morning to noon, the water police tried their best to clear the waterway, but it was still not possible to pass. It is now reported that the ships on both sides have been ordered to retreat, and it may be possible to clear the waterway today, but it is still uncertain.

Impact on Ferries. Due to the blockage of the waterway, many ferries were unable to operate. Larger inland river vessels with scheduled routes temporarily changed their routes to travel along the outer river, which is farther than the inner river. The most affected were the cargo and passenger ships from the inland areas that came to Shanghai to sell goods, as they were blocked and unable to enter. There were also many who loaded goods to leave Shanghai but were unable to leave the river, resulting in significant losses.

The Shanghai National Goods Company's Second Plan is Active

Amidst Weak Purchasing Power

The Company is Not Affected

Since the enemy's invasion of Shanghai on January 28th, all industries have been affected, resulting in a general economic downturn in society. This month, as winter approaches and the weather is slightly colder, social purchasing power is even weaker. The Shanghai National Goods Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, decided to hold a large-scale promotion of women's national goods, starting on the 6th of this month, as part of its second plan for the year. The goods selected are of high quality and the prices are low, which is unprecedented. Therefore, although social purchasing power is weak, the company's daily sales statistics are not affected, and are increasing daily. The total sales on the 11th exceeded the daily target by 196.38%. Sales from the 12th onwards exceeded by 125.08%. The average increase for the two days was over 160%, which is even better than the average for the past five days. The reason is that those who love to buy national goods trust companies that completely sell national goods and do not have any concerns. Another reason is that the company introduces inexpensive and beautiful goods to women in separate sessions and departments, which can indeed sacrifice profits and attract buyers. For example, today's sale of 6.8 jiao per foot of genuine silk patriotic crepe, 3.5 jiao per pound of Guangdong first-class kapok, 1.4 jiao per foot of floral line riding pants, 5 jiao each for a domestic brand thermos, 5 pairs for one yuan of double-thread men's socks, 5.5 jiao each for a Guan Le Ming fountain pen, 9.5 jiao each for a Ya Pu Er electric bulb, 4.8 yuan each for a children's coat, and a buy-one-get-one-free Bakelite appliance set are all genuine sacrifices and low-priced goods.

Mutual Election of Standing Committee Members, Chairman and Vice-Chairman

And Discussion of the Chinese Businessmen's Self-Defense Corps Issue

The French Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association held its first Executive Committee meeting of the third session yesterday at 2:00 PM inside the Shandong Guild Hall on Ximen Road. The following committee members were present: Zhou Qinpu, Cheng Zhusun, Li Weiliang, Dong Kechang, Wang Shunqing, Du Gang, Mao Yun, Du Yuesheng, (Cheng represented by) Bei Zairong, Xu Xiuting, Wu Xiu, (Du represented by) Huang Degu, (Wang represented by) Cai Hongtian, (Mao represented by) Zhu Shengmao, Shang Mujiang, (Zhu represented by) Tong Lizhang, Qu Zhenhua, Gong Jingyan, (Qu represented by), 18 people. Cheng Zhusun was publicly elected as Chairman, and Shao Bing was the recorder. After formalities, the Chairman gave a report, stating that the purpose of today's meeting was to mutually elect the Chairman, Vice-Chairman, and Standing Committee members. Because the number of executive committee members has increased by four in this session, and the number of Standing Committee members was five in the previous session, the number should be increased by two to a total of seven. The proposal was unanimously approved without dissent. Next, Zhang Gengshan, representing Wu Guowei, proposed that anyone elected as a Chinese Director or Chinese Committee member, whose duties are already burdensome, should not concurrently hold positions as Executive or Supervisory Committee members of this association. The Chairman put the matter to discussion. Li Weiliang, Shao Baoxing, and others seconded the motion. It was resolved that the opinions would be handed over to the committee responsible for drafting amendments to the regulations. Next, there was a discussion about alternate committee members attending meetings and being able to perform the duties of formal committee members when they are absent, with responsibility limited to one occasion. After Mao Yun explained the above opinion, there was no dissent. The Chairman stated that amending the regulations was of utmost importance, and a number of drafting committee members should be appointed first. It was resolved to publicly elect Cheng Zhusun, Qu Zhenhua, Huang Xianggu, Mao Yun, and Tong Lizhang as members of the committee. Next, Wang Shunqing proposed to revive the Chinese Businessmen's Self-Defense Corps. After the Chairman reported on the preparation process in detail, Mao Yun, Qu Zhenhua, Tong Lizhang, Li Weiliang, and others successively advocated that the Self-Defense Corps must be established. It was resolved to first, based on the original plan prepared last time, send a letter to the French authorities, inquiring about the reasons why the establishment has not yet been approved. The letter should also detail that the French Concession was the first to advocate the establishment, and now the Public Concession has approved the establishment of a Special Police Chinese Corps, which has achieved excellent results so far. This is sufficient to show that this type of organization does not conflict with the government's administration, and it is beneficial to local business without any harm. Similarly, the past Chinese Volunteer Corps in the French Concession also had good results. It seems there is no harm in starting implementation as soon as possible. However, all implementation methods, in addition to the existing basic members (i.e., members of the Chinese Volunteer Corps), will be discussed and implemented in detail once formal approval is obtained. Next, Li Weiliang reported on the theft case at the Yonghua Company on Xinxiao Street, French Avenue. It was unanimously agreed that, as it is the dead of winter and there are many thieves, in addition to requesting protection from the French authorities, citizens within the concession should be notified to pay attention to prevention. After the above cases were discussed, the mutual election of the Chairman and Standing Committee members began. Du Yuesheng was elected as Chairman, and Cheng Zhusun and Shang Mujiang were elected as Vice-Chairmen, all of whom were re-elected. Xu Xiuting, Qu Zhenhua, Mao Yun, Huang Xianggu, Li Weiliang, Zhu Shengmao, and Gong Jingyan were elected as Standing Committee members. It was also decided that the inauguration and oath-taking ceremony for the Chinese Directors, Chinese Committee members, and Executive and Supervisory Committee members would be held within the 20th of this month. The date will be determined by Chairman Du. The meeting adjourned at around 6:00 PM.

After the Recovery of Xiamen, Chinese Merchants' Ships Resume Sailing

However, Passenger and Cargo Volumes Sharply Decline Due to the Impact of War

Since the Fujian Incident, all Chinese merchant shipping companies have, according to the order of the Ministry of Transportation, uniformly stopped sailing to ports in Fujian Province, such as Fuzhou, Xiamen, Xinghua, Quanzhou, Shacheng, etc. However, foreign merchant ships continue to sail as usual, resulting in the monopolization of passenger and cargo transportation by foreign ships. For example, the Jiesheng, which sails on the Shanghai-Fuzhou line, has excellent business on each voyage from Fuzhou to Shanghai. Now that Xiamen has been recovered by the Navy, Chinese merchant ships can resume sailing to Xiamen as usual. The Yuan'an, which was scheduled to sail the Nanhua route from Shanghai yesterday by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, originally planned to dock at Xiamen. However, because passenger and cargo traffic from Shanghai to Xiamen has disappeared since the Fujian Incident, and cargo from Xiamen to Shanghai has also sharply declined, it still stopped docking. Whether it will dock at Xiamen when returning to Shanghai from Guangdong depends on whether there are passengers and cargo at Xiamen at that time.

Labor Strike at the Old Tin Packaging Plant of the British American Tobacco Company

The Labor Union Petitions the Party and Government for Mediation

According to the Da Gong News Agency, the workers in the tin packaging section of the old factory of the British American Tobacco Company in Pudong recently went on strike due to the factory's change of closing time and confiscation of worker ID cards. Yesterday, they went on strike as usual and will be able to work as usual tomorrow. The details are as follows:

The Truth About the Labor Strike

The tin packaging section of the old factory of the British American Tobacco Company in Lujiazui employs more than 100 long-term workers and about 1,000 temporary female workers. Traditionally, they enter the factory at 7:00 AM every day and leave for lunch at 11:45 AM, returning to work at 12:50 PM. Recently, the factory changed the lunch break to 11:50 AM. The workers expressed dissatisfaction with the sudden change. The day before yesterday, after the female workers went for lunch, they entered the factory at around 12:00 PM, but unexpectedly, the boxes for the worker ID cards were removed. After the workers entered the factory, they could not work because they had no ID cards, so they had to leave the factory as a whole and report to the labor union. Negotiations by the labor union were still unsuccessful. At 5:00 PM, a general meeting of the tin packaging workers was held, and it was decided that (yesterday, Saturday, was a day off) starting from Monday, they would enter the factory to work as usual and would not recognize the factory's change of time.

Petition for Mediation

The Fifth District Cigarette Industry Labor Union, on the grounds that the factory changed working hours and confiscated work cards, leading to disputes, has now decided through a general meeting to start working as usual on Monday, but the working hours will still follow the old practice. Fearing that the factory will change again and cause disputes, they specially petitioned the Municipal Party Department Social Affairs Bureau yesterday to request the dispatch of personnel for mediation to avoid disturbances.

The Copper and Iron Industry Association Dispatches Personnel to Seal Off Smuggled Iron

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Xiangfeng Foundry in this city was previously found to be using smuggled iron and was warned by the Copper and Iron Industry Association. Later, it was found that this smuggled iron was from Xiangtai Ironworks. After Xiangfeng was warned by the association, it did not mend its ways and continued to use smuggled iron, which was again discovered by the association. Xiangtai and Xiangfeng, as well as the Iron Industry Association, were invited to discuss and resolve that the smuggled iron would be sealed off. In the future, all members of the same industry would not be allowed to use it. Unexpectedly, Xiangfeng outwardly complied but secretly continued to use the smuggled iron. The association believed that Xiangfeng was a member of the same industry and had the right to interfere. The association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting a resolution. The Copper and Iron Industry Association specially held a regular meeting at 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, and most of the committee members raised the issue of how to deal with Xiangfeng Foundry, which ignored the advice, repeatedly violated the resolution, and privately used smuggled iron. It was resolved to recommend committee member Zhang Zilian to contact the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting the dispatch of personnel to weigh and seal off the smuggled iron to ensure prudence and avoid repeating the mistakes.

Youth Association Lecture "The Way Out for Young People" Lecture Two

The theme of this year's moral education lecture at the Shanghai Youth Association is "The Way Out for Young People." The theme is divided into four lectures, all given by famous people, as reported in this newspaper. The topic of the second lecture is "The Standard of New Morality," and Dr. Jin Wuzhou will be giving the lecture at 4:00 PM today (the 14th) in the auditorium of the association in the Eight Immortals Bridge. Young men and women from all walks of life who have new ideas should attend at that time. It will surely be a refreshing experience, so don't miss it.

Chinese Take Over Laodeji Soda Factory

No. 94 Yulin Road, the Laodeji Dutch Water Factory, was founded by Westerners and has a history of 80 years. It is the pioneer of soda in China and holds Business License No. 1 from the Shanghai Municipal Council. In the beginning, it only provided drinks for people in the west of Shanghai. Later, many Chinese people also drank it. The various sodas it produces, with their excellent materials, appropriate ingredients, and fresh and delicious taste, are indeed superior to all other brands on the market. However, in recent years, the successors of the founders are old and frail and have no intention of promoting it, so it is rarely sold on the market except to Westerners. Last year, it was taken over by Chinese who raised funds to acquire it and renamed it Laodeji Soda Company. An office was added on the third floor of the Jiangnan Bank on Paoqiu Chang Road, Henan Road. All the original technicians and employees, who had been with the Westerners for twenty or thirty years, remained. After the takeover, this reporter was invited by technician Mr. Liu of the company to visit. The layout of its machinery and various equipment are more complete than other factories. Its factory building is also specially constructed, which is unmatched by other factories. The water used is filtered through sand and then sterilized with ultraviolet light to kill bacteria. The spices are all from a factory in England. After the empty bottles are washed inside and out by machine, they are rinsed with distilled water. After the soda is bottled, each bottle is inspected, and any water with minute dust particles is discarded and not sold. No effort is spared in ensuring hygiene, so it has been able to thrive for eighty years without failing. The company is determined to work hard to promote and step up production this spring so that Chinese people can drink top-quality domestic soda. This is also good news in the national products industry.

Zhongxin Socks Factory Burnt Down Last Night

At 6:30 PM last night, the Zhongxin Socks Factory at No. 4, Lane 5, Zhaojiawan, in the jurisdiction of the First Precinct, First Sub-Bureau of the Nanshi Public Security Bureau, suddenly suffered an accident and quickly caught fire. Fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm and tried their best to extinguish the fire. It took an hour to put it out. After an investigation into the cause of the fire, it was found that the factory's old servant, Xu Yindi, was careless while cooking dinner, causing the fire. The fire destroyed a two-story building and a large overhanging building, resulting in significant losses.

Japanese Man Injures Three People While Driving

At around 9:00 AM yesterday morning, a certain Japanese man drove a motorized bicycle at lightning speed through the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Laobazi Road. Three people happened to be crossing the road, and the car was unable to stop in time, knocking them all to the ground. All three were seriously injured. Later, a Chinese police officer saw it and immediately sent the injured people and car to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The Japanese man who caused the accident was detained in the police station pending interrogation. The names of the injured people are as follows: Ding Shouchun, 36 years old, from Jiangbei, injured in the abdomen; Ye Wu, 30 years old, from Jiangbei, injured in both feet; Luo Yongquan, 57 years old, from Ningbo, injured in the head. It is said that Luo Yongquan was the most seriously injured and his life may be in danger.

China Land Reclamation Bank Inspection Report

China Land Reclamation Bank's report on the inspection of reserve funds for banknotes issued states that the bank's issue and operating reserves have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve is above 70% and the guarantee reserve is below 30%. On the 13th of this month, after an inspection by accountant Wang Zikang, together with Xu Jiqu, Xu Busun, representatives of the board of directors, the results were as follows: the total amount of banknotes issued was 6,445,000 silver dollars. The total amount of reserve funds for banknotes issued was 6,445,000 silver dollars, including a cash reserve of 5,071,000 silver dollars and a guarantee reserve of 1,374,000 silver dollars. The above two items indicate that the cash reserve accounts for slightly less than 79% and the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly more than 2%. This is a special report. January 13, year 23.

Reading Q&A

Regarding Choosing a Subject to Study [>P

Several Questions about Purpose (Continued)

In many applications, a person often lists three or four, or even five or six, or more subjects to study. For example, wanting to study both literature and science, as well as other subjects such as architecture and automotive engineering. Whether studying several subjects at the same time will conflict and reduce efficiency is a question that remains to be discussed, but due to limited time, if one studies several subjects at the same time, the result will inevitably be neglecting one thing for another, achieving nothing. We dare to assert this. Regarding this point, Mr. Shao Guoquan's letter of inquiry is proof: "...Fortunately, the working hours of my job are very few, only five hours on average per day... So I study English at your newspaper's night school and Chinese at a certain society. But after a semester, studying two subjects seems to be mentally taxing, resulting in no progress. Speaking of my personality, I like both Chinese and English equally, and I need them equally in my career. Sir, in this situation, should I give up one, or continue with both simultaneously?" Our reply to Mr. Shao is: "If you find it difficult to study both, then rather than forcing yourself to continue, neglecting one for the other, it is better to focus on one subject and gain more benefit." If someone with as much free time as Mr. Shao still feels this difficulty, the harm of studying multiple subjects can be imagined. Therefore, we hope that participants who like to study several subjects at the same time should first choose the one they like the most and need the most.

It is a fact that mastering a language is a prerequisite for learning, especially in China, because of its cultural backwardness. Studying science requires reading foreign books. Therefore, learning a foreign language has become the main subject in today's schools, the prerequisite for reading. However, learning a foreign language takes at least two or three years, and even then, one may not be able to master it. Therefore, while learning a foreign language is extremely necessary, one also needs to consider their own learning environment. Therefore, many participants intend to learn a foreign language in order to read social sciences or natural sciences. Regarding this, we believe that two prerequisite questions must be resolved: (1) Is there enough time? (2) Is it for specialized research or just to gain general knowledge? If it is only to gain general knowledge and there is not enough time, then learning a foreign language is largely unnecessary. Because if one spends too much time learning a foreign language, and as a result, the foreign language is not mastered and the subject one wants to read is not learned at all, it is the most uneconomical thing. Moreover, this issue can be discussed from two aspects. Social sciences in China seem to be more developed than natural sciences in recent times, and there are quite a few translated books and newspapers in terms of quantity, enough for those of us who only want to understand practical life to study.

As we were writing this article, we received a letter from Mr. Yu Wanwang, who raised the question of "Which is more important, natural science or social science?" We have a lot to say about this question and will discuss it separately tomorrow. We will put it aside for now.

In conclusion: Although we have a considerable understanding of the readers' learning environment, we cannot directly and bluntly let readers learn a certain subject. We can only, according to their living environment, suggest how to make the books they read beneficial, not futile, and not take unnecessary detours. As for which subject to choose to study, it should still be proposed by the reader in a "study plan." However, we are willing to be in the position of an observer, to discuss the proposed plan and do our best to fulfill the responsibility of an "experienced guide."

Shen Huichun Assault Incident: Court to Hold Hearing Tomorrow at 2:00 PM Still at the District Court

During the Jiaotong University, Jinan University, and Jiangnan University football match, referee Shen Huichun was assaulted by Jiaotong University students. Shen hired lawyer Yan Ersen last week to file a lawsuit in the District Court. A preliminary hearing has already been held once. However, the prosecutor ordered Shen to file a lawsuit in the Special District Court because the Jiaotong University campus is located on an extraterritorial road. However, Shen argued that although the Jiaotong University gate is on an extraterritorial road, the police authority is still in the hands of the Public Security Bureau. The District Court then agreed to accept the case and is now scheduled to hold a hearing tomorrow at 2:00 PM.

Cheers Erupt at the Baseball Field: Donghua Defeats Huasaises Again 1-2. Both Sides' Artistic Performances are Wonderful and Exciting. The Focus of Victory Depends on Accurate Shooting. Western Concession Police Force Loses to French Business School 1-2.

In the Western League Group A competition, Donghua had previously defeated Huasaises by a score of 2-1. Yesterday afternoon, the two teams played their second Western League Group A match at the baseball field. In front of 5,000 spectators, they fought fiercely for ninety minutes. As a result, Donghua defeated Huasaises again by the same score of 2-1. Huasaises, who were regarded highly in Shanghai, were also willing to submit at this time and had to dejectedly pack up their remaining forces and leave.

Deliberately Seeking Strength and Restoring Fame

Donghua suffered a setback at the hands of Jinan University last week, and their fame was greatly damaged. Those in charge gathered everyone to discuss the aftermath. In order to strive for revival, they relied on reorganizing the team. After the swearing-in ceremony, they indeed increased training every day. The strength of the troops was strengthened, and the spirit was enhanced. Even strong enemies like Huasaises were defeated. If this continues, Donghua should be watched with new eyes. Looking at the situation on that day, the forwards ran and passed, while the opponent excelled in internal defense and resistance. Donghua was more stable. The focus of the victory or defeat of both sides lay in the number of people who were good at shooting. The British troops had A Qiao alone, while Donghua had Dai and Li. When the opportunity came, the outcome was different.

Yunyou's Appearance Brings a Fresh Atmosphere

Donghua's recent setbacks were due to the entire army's laxity. The absence of midfielder Feng Yunyou due to illness was also one of the reasons. Yesterday, Mr. Feng took the field to fight. Although he was weak after his illness, he still worked hard and cooperated with the heroes. Coupled with the amazing performances of Tu Kaiyuan and Wu Youliang, the midfield line felt vibrant. Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, and Guan Xun'an's skills are superb, and everyone knows it. Wan Xianghua and Jia Youliang each had wonderful crosses. The two were accurate and skillful in shooting. It is now increasingly believed that those who ran all over the field and chased the ball tirelessly were Tu Kaiyuan on the inside and Chen Hongguang on the outside.

The Enemy's Formation is Tidy, but Shooting is Poor

Huasaises' second defeat at the hands of Donghua was probably beyond their expectations. The closeness of the entire team's cooperation and the strength of the front and rear offense and defense were sometimes better than Donghua's. The only drawback was that the forwards lacked shooting talent compared to Donghua. Often, when they were at the city gates, they panicked and didn't know what to do, shooting aimlessly everywhere. Goalkeeper Herbert was a first-class talent. The two goals conceded were beyond human ability, but the number of saves he made was more than double the number of goals conceded, so his contribution was enough to offset the losses. Tao Lewei, the veteran, had an imposing manner. Smith, the midfielder, was indeed extraordinary. The five forwards ran fast and passed well, but only A Qiao could shoot.

The Enemy Gains Momentum, Donghua is in Trouble

After the whistle blew to start the battle, Huasaises immediately launched a full-scale attack on Donghua's defense. Feng Yunyou, who was fighting while ill, tried his best to defend, but both attempts were ineffective. Li Yichen and Xiao Wan launched a counterattack in succession, but were intercepted by Smith. Kang Budeng and A Qiao gained momentum and came again. Li Ning waved them out of the door. A Qiao was the only dangerous person on the other side, galloping on horseback on Donghua's back line. Fortunately, Lao Zhou's hands and feet were steady, and he was not poisoned. Huasaises' forwards attacked repeatedly but did not lose heart because of it. They gathered around Donghua's penalty area and attacked repeatedly. Tu and Wu, two defenders, rescued dangerous balls one after another. Li Ning was magnificent, and the enemy was frightened when they saw him.

Youliang Penetrates Deeply, Linjing's Contribution

After a long time of back and forth, it was still difficult to open the scoring. Guan Xun'an rescued a dangerous ball, picking and sending it to the center. Smith headed it back. Feng Yunyou hooked it sideways, and Hongguang got it. He took a few steps forward, and Weston rushed at him in a shocking manner. Hongguang was cunning and passed it to Jia. Jia dribbled the ball straight down, breaking through three levels. Tao Lewei entangled desperately, but slipped and fell, causing a catastrophic disaster. The ball was hooked by Jia in front of the goal. Agerton and Harickton misunderstood each other. The center forward Dai took the opportunity to rush forward a few steps and kicked it in with a bang. Cheers erupted from all around. Donghua led 1-0 in the first half.

A Qiao Shoots Angrily, Tying the Score

Time passed, and the war drums sounded again. After switching defenses, Donghua suddenly found themselves in an attacking position. However, Smith was very powerful, monitoring Dai and not leaving him for a moment. Li Yichen could not break through and dribble in, so he shot from 30 yards away. It was extremely accurate. Herbert fell to the ground and pushed it out, avoiding a major disaster. Ten minutes later, Kang Budeng and A Qiao, under Smith's orders, galloped away, arriving at Donghua's defense in an instant. Wu Youliang could not stop them, and Guan Xun'an could not block them again. In the penalty area, shadows were chaotic. A Qiao, relying on his strong feet, shot angrily. Zhou's iron gate's line of sight was blocked by people, so it became a tie.

Xianghua Cheers, Yichen Unleashes His Power

Since the situation was balanced

, the battle became more intense. Xianghua got the ball as fast as a galloping horse, and Harick could not catch up. Agterton was tricked in front, and the ball flew along the low line in front of the goal. Dai Linjing was unprepared in a hurry, so he missed this good opportunity. There was a sigh from all around. A Scene from an Important Hong Kong Football Group A Match: South China Defeats Lincoln 1-0. Previously Lost 1-2, Now Wins 1-0. However, Although South China Wins, There are Still Many Thorns in Their Path to Hegemony. China Loses to Welsh 1-2.

(Hong Kong News) In the previous match between the South China Group A football team and the Lincoln team, South China was defeated by a score of 1-2. Therefore, the championship issue was greatly affected. And yesterday, Sunday (the 7th), the two teams met again. Old enemies meeting are especially clear-eyed. As a result, South China won 1-0 in the last three minutes due to their better formation, washing away the shame of their previous defeat. On that day, the Caroline You Football Field attracted no less than several thousand Hong Kong and Chinese fans due to the prestige of the two teams. The grand occasion was rarely seen in the past. This shows the importance of this match's victory or defeat. On the South China side, Li Guowei was injured, and Tang Kun filled the vacancy. Huang Jiliang was unable to play due to matters, and Bao Jiaping filled the role of goalkeeper. The strength was not reduced compared to the original formation. The Lincoln team's members remained the same. Only the goalkeeper and two defenders were promoted from Group B, so the defense was inevitably weaker. Judging from the performances of the two teams on that day, South China was slightly better than Lincoln. Bao Jiaping and Li Tiansheng saved many dangerous balls. Tang Kun was the bravest, once blocking the enemy team's right forward from dribbling the ball close to the goal and shooting. The situation was extremely dangerous, but Tang blocked the ball with his body. His contribution was truly great. Forward Feng Jingxiang was monitored by the enemy's defender, so although he was very successful in the first half, he could not win due to a lack of support. The audience praised Ji Liang and Shui Yi's legs and Jiang Bai's head. Only Li Shuoyou, who had just arrived in Hong Kong from Shanghai, lacked connection with the other players due to the initial collaboration, and his performance was slightly less brilliant. It is believed that Li will naturally become more proficient as he collaborates with the other players for a longer time. Lincoln's forwards were also extremely strong, comparable to South China. Although the goalkeeper was a latecomer, he was also quite competent. The main reason for their failure was the weakness of the defenders. Although South China won this time, there are still many thorns in the future. If they can move forward bravely and unstoppable, then this year's championship may be won again.

South China Takes the Offensive First

South China kicked off, and Lincoln center forward Higgins rushed forward to snatch the ball. South China's three center backs rushed forward to support and quickly passed it to Lincoln's territory, with great prestige, making Lincoln's defense see and lose heart. Lincoln's goalkeeper opened the goal kick, and the five forwards worked hard to attack. However, they failed to break through South China's defense line three times in a row. Even if they managed to advance to the territory, they would definitely be repelled by Li Tiansheng. Before long, Li Tiansheng got the ball. Lie Li rushed to snatch it, feeling quite successful. However, Bao Jiaping made a wonderful move, and Lie Li could do nothing. Bao passed the goal kick to the center, and Shui Yi galloped away. Liang Rongzhao saw the opportunity and passed it. Yang Shuiyi then had the opportunity to go one-on-one. Zheng Jiliang also accelerated and advanced. Lincoln could not support it and conceded a corner kick first. Shui Yi kicked it. The landing point was excellent. Tan Jiangxi was supposed to assist on the left, but at some point, he had sneaked to the right and charged up, sending the ball towards the goal. However, his strength was not enough, so it was saved by Dejin. Otherwise, South China would have been able to win a goal first and gain an advantage at this time.

Still Unable to Fulfill His Wish

South China was eager to win and besieged again, fighting fiercely in front of the Lincoln formation. Tan Jiangbai shot too hard, and the ball flew wildly away. Lincoln's siege began to be lifted. At that time, the South China troops were concentrated in the front and did not defend against Lie Li and He Jia's coordinated attack, causing South China to retreat step by step. Li Tiansheng witnessed the enemy troops on the road, as if entering an uninhabited territory, so he asked to come out again, cut off Lie and He's connection, and passed it to the front. Shui Yi made a wonderful pass, and the ball landed at the twelve-yard spot. Feng Jingxiang, Zheng Jiliang, and Tan Jiangbai swarmed in. The Lincoln formation was extremely dangerous. However, Lincoln was very lucky. Although the South China forwards fell and shot repeatedly, they were able to defend the last line of defense. The virgin membrane was not broken by South China.

Suspected of Getting a Penalty Kick

South China had not achieved results by advancing from the right for a long time, so they ordered Li Shiyou to be the main force for the advance, dribbling the ball forward, extremely agile. Therefore, South China poured out its troops again. Unfortunately, the first half had ended at this time. Although South China had its back to the sun in the second half, Lincoln used skirmishers to intercept South China's attacking troops and seize the opportunity to attack the goal. Although they could not win, they still made South China worry. After fifteen minutes, South China was able to develop slightly, but Dejin was able to safely save all the dangerous balls. At that time, South China advanced from the left more often, but Li Shiyou and Tan Jiangbai did not cooperate well, and their performance was not excellent. At 25 minutes, the two armies fought in a mixed battle at the twelve-yard spot in front of the Lincoln formation. You came and I went, in great chaos. The referee's whistle suddenly sounded. The audience thought that Lincoln must have been penalized with a twelve-yard free kick. While hesitating, Lincoln's Rowton quickly picked up the ball and kicked it out. The audience then knew that the Chinese team had been penalized.

Shui Yi is Ambitious

Then, Lincoln's right assistant, the burly MacKinney, had the ball passed to him, so he took a few steps forward and passed it to He Jia remotely. He Jia dribbled the ball, invaded the pass, and in an instant, the blond strongman had arrived in front of the formation. He Jia carefully crossed with his left foot. MacKinney was about to raise his foot and tap it, but Tang Kun's healthy feet arrived first and turned the danger into safety. Then, Yang Shuiyi was ambitious and got the ball and attacked the goal. The left center back, Bi Tuo, tried his best to defend, but Yang Shuiyi rushed past him. When he reached the last line of defense, he lost his hand and Imeson kicked the ball out. If Shuiyi could have advanced a few more yards, then Lincoln would have had no luck at this time. The entire South China team fought hard, but the results were almost zero. At this point, all the personnel of the team were very anxious. And because Li Shiyou was running for South China for the first time, the mysteries of which may not be clear, Tan Jiangbai could not fully develop his strengths. Fortunately, Jiang Bai's ambition to advance was never lazy, so he was able to win in the last two minutes.

Jiang Bai Makes a Contribution with His Head

The strongest defender on Lincoln's side that day

was definitely the center back, Queshi, who almost gave Feng Jingxiang no chance to shoot. Among the inside forwards, only Zheng Jiliang and Tan Jiangbai could move around slightly. At this time, South China ignored the consequences and abandoned the rear in order to win first. As expected, the opportunity to win the ball had arrived. Zheng Jiliang sent a ball, and Tan Jiangbai met it with his head. The onlookers were very clear-eyed and saw that the ball was already in the net and the enemy's goal had fallen. The onlookers applauded and stomped their feet, overjoyed. In the end, South China avenged themselves with a score of 1-0, washing away the shame of their previous defeat.
