The Final Reckoning of 1933 (Part 1)

A Miniature of International Politics in 1933

— Ms. Luo Jie

1933 was the fifth year of the capitalist world's panic. In this year, the world's imperialists racked their brains to implement all measures to overcome the panic: they held the World Economic Conference, they built high tariff barriers, they implemented inflation, they chanted the "controlled" economy, and they put forward countless "revival" plans... However, in the melee of "revival," "control," tariffs, and currency, the panic developed more deeply and more widely: the army of unemployed people was flooding like a flood, the imbalance between production and consumption broke past records, and the financial chaos exceeded the levels of previous years since the panic.

Departing from this deep and broad wave of panic, unfolded the tense, dangerous, complex, intricate, kaleidoscope-like international politics of 1933:

First, the bankruptcy of the League of Nations—the League of Nations, an imperialist spoils-sharing conference, could no longer maintain their superficial "alliance" and carry out their deception of spreading "peace" and "assistance" in 1933, when conflicts between imperialists were extremely sharp and the war of redistributing colonies was imminent. Japanese imperialism, in order to facilitate its own exclusive rule over Manchuria and North China, even found this superficial "constraint" a bit annoying, and was the first to tear off this paper-thin mask and "withdraw from the League of Nations"! The Four-Power Pact of Britain, France, Italy, and Germany, although it wanted to ease the conflict between imperialists in Europe and strengthen the anti-Soviet Union front, still could not stop German imperialism from firing a second shot at the League of Nations: "Withdraw from the League of Nations"! This fully illustrates that in 1933, the imperialists could no longer carry out the sharing of spoils in "peace," and were already sharpening their swords and preparing for a second large-scale plundering massacre.

Second, the strengthening of imperialist economic blocs—the complete failure of the London World Economic Conference led to the further strengthening of the economic blocs (Bloc Economies) of various imperialists. Britain, the United States, France, and Japan each possessed their directly controlled territories, colonies, and spheres of influence, implemented high tariff barriers, lowered exchange rates, and used trade reciprocity to protect their own commodity markets and exclude foreign commodities. They used all means to unfold the spectacle of a world market economic war. This is directly the prelude to military war!

Third, the intensification of the imperialist arms race:—The fact that the Geneva Disarmament Conference has become an arms expansion conference has concretely explained this fact. Germany's demand for military equality, Britain, Japan, the United States, France, and Italy's desperate expansion of armaments, the increase in the military budgets of various imperialist countries, and the unprecedented prosperity of the military industry are concrete evidence of this fact.

Fourth, the universality of the political Fascistization of imperialism—Hitler took control of the German regime at the beginning of 1933, and is now the pillar to maintain the last fate of German capitalism; the Fascistization of the Japanese ruling class has become the last watchman of the capitalist world in the Far East, and the Roosevelt's movement in the United States, and the "controlled economy" of various imperialists, are all actually fascist tendencies. This further intensifies the conflicts between imperialists, intensifies the exploitation and oppression of workers and colonies and semi-colonies, and makes the war crisis and the revolutionary crisis more and more urgent.

Fifth, the upsurge of the world anti-imperialist movement—the anti-imperialist struggle of the working class in various imperialist countries has had a wide-ranging development this year. The radicalization of the British Independent Labour Party's actions, and the establishment of the anti-capitalist and anti-fascist united movements of the laboring masses in the United States, France, Italy, Germany, and other capitalist countries, are concrete explanations. In addition, the turmoil in Cuba and Luo Luo, and the development of revolutionary movements in South America, Africa, India, and other places, have all had significant phenomena in 1933.

Sixth, the Soviet Union in 1933—1933 was the second year of the implementation of the Soviet Union's second five-year plan. The gradual progress of socialist construction in Soviet Russia, and the gradual success of its peaceful diplomacy: the signing of the multilateral non-aggression treaty by the Black Sea and Baltic Sea coastal countries, the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia and the United States and Russia, established another milestone in the international politics of this year.

1933 was the year when all imperialist countries in the capitalist world attempted to jointly attack the Soviet Union to solve their own contradictions, but were defeated by the Soviet Union's "peaceful policy"; 1933 was the year when the contradictions and conflicts between imperialists intensified, and everyone sharpened their swords and prepared for slaughter. At the same time, it was also the year when the imperialists intensified the carving up of the world's masses and prepared to use them as cannon fodder.

The Anglo-Japanese Economic War of 1933

— Ms. Lu Xiaodai

Britain is an old capitalist country, a predecessor of imperialism, and the world's largest trader. "The British Empire never sets," which means the vastness of the British Empire's colonies, the breadth of the British Empire's world market, and the pride of the British Empire.

However, after the European War, the rapid advancement of American imperialism shook the foundation of the British Empire in the entire world market. In the past two or three years, the leap of the emerging Japanese imperialism has also posed a serious threat to the British Empire's main markets.

The main exports of Japanese imperialism are raw silk, cotton textiles, and rayon. Except for raw silk, cotton textiles and rayon are important exports of the British Empire. This has determined the fierce competition between British and Japanese imperialism in the world market. At the same time, most of the customers for Japanese imperialist cotton textiles and rayon are dominions and colonies of the British Empire. In addition, due to Japan's advanced production technology and cheap labor – which means that Japanese capitalists severely exploit workers – its costs are generally lower than those of Britain; the sharp fall in the Japanese yen gives it an absolute advantage in foreign markets; at the same time, the forcible occupation of Manchuria further supports the spine of Japanese imperialism, and vigorously implements a policy of devaluation and sales (dumping) to foreign countries. As a result, Japanese goods poured into the British Empire's market, launching a desperate economic war between British and Japanese imperialism in 1933!

The main battlefields of the Anglo-Japanese economic war are India, the Straits Settlements, Africa, the Near East, and China. It is clear that the British Empire is adopting a difficult defensive posture, while Japanese imperialism is taking a very fierce offensive.

India is one of the largest colonies of the British Empire and one of its largest treasures. However, British goods in the Indian market are all feeling the pressure and extreme blows of Japanese goods, especially the decline of British cotton cloth is even more significant. The amount of Japanese cotton cloth imported into India has exceeded the amount imported into India from Britain itself. | Japan 650 million yards, Britain only 600 million yards.

In the Straits Settlements, the Dutch East Indies, Turkey and the Near East, Egypt and other African colonies, the same can be seen with the entry and exit of Japanese goods, and the decline of British goods. In Australia and China, although British goods show a trend of development, Japanese goods still rush in like a tide, especially in northern and central China, Japan still occupies an overwhelming advantage.

The panic of the entire capitalist world became even deeper and wider in 1933. Seeing that the overseas market was becoming increasingly narrow, the British Empire naturally could not remain silent and wait for death. Therefore, it mobilized all the territories and dominions of the British Empire, continued the spirit of the Ottawa Conference in June 1932, implemented a counter-attack against Japan, and built high tariff barriers in India, Egypt, Australia, the Straits Settlements, and other African dominions, increasing dumping taxes to prevent the inflow of Japanese goods, and using preferential tariffs to maintain the British goods’ foothold.

Japan is not showing weakness either. When the British colonies, especially India, raised tariffs and abandoned the Japan-India Trade Agreement, Japanese textile capitalists declared a boycott of Indian cotton; at the same time, at the World Economic Conference, the Japanese representatives blatantly declared an anti-British attitude; and further implemented retaliatory tariffs on British goods within the Japanese economic system.

The Anglo-Japanese economic war has intensified! The World Economic Conference had no effect on reconciliation; the Japan-India Simla Conference could not ease their conflict either!

In China, the British Empire is unfolding its fan shape from Hong Kong, implementing an attempt to monopolize South China. However, Japanese goods are still constantly rushing into South China; at the same time, Japan is using Manchuria as a base to unfold a wider fan shape in North China. The Yangtze River area in Central China is an even more contested place for Britain and Japan, the location of the duel.

The Anglo-Japanese imperialist economic war is very sensitive and inevitably reflected in the diplomatic war. The breakdown of the World Economic Conference, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, and the shelving of the disarmament conference all indicate the contradictions and conflicts between imperialists, and the opposition between Britain and Japan has also become sharply apparent.

1933 was a year in which the Anglo-Japanese economic war intensified. However, the past of 1933 did not take away the contradictions and conflicts between British and Japanese imperialism, but only deepened with the arrival of 1934!

The inherent contradictions of capitalism are destined to make British and Japanese imperialists unable to stop their economic competition. The result of their competition is to make the panic of the capitalist world even deeper, to increase the exploitation of the working masses in their respective countries, and to make the oppression of the colonies even more cruel! Finally, it will transform from economic war into military war between imperialists!

Their Marriage Will Never Break Up

— Siying

Everyone said that their marriage would not last, but they have not shown any signs of breaking up so far. They are still loving each other, and the longer it lasts, the stronger it becomes. In the film industry of Hollywood, almost everyone thinks this is a very strange thing. The rumour-mongers of Hollywood's divorce industry can no longer use their skills. Who are these two? They are Ann Dvorak and Leslie Fenton, not obscure figures either. Ann Dvorak recently played the leading role in "The Way to Love". That film was originally starred by Sylvia Sidney, the lead actress of "Madame Butterfly" this year. She stopped acting halfway through, so the company borrowed Ann Dvorak from Warner Brothers to play the leading role. This is a very glorious thing for Ann Dvorak. As for Leslie Fenton, he has also played the leading role in many big films in Germany, so he is not without status.

Before they got married, everyone gave them a nickname. Leslie was called "Bad Boy" and Ann? Called "Wonder Girl". Their status, thoughts, and ages were not the same in any way. Their love was just a temporary impulse, without any deep feelings. Therefore, when they were about to announce their engagement, Ann's mother was afraid that their marriage would not last, so she advised them not to act rashly and to wait as friends for at least a year. Ann's mother herself was a stage performer, and she knew the difficulty of balancing marriage and career, and especially feared that their romance would not last. One was a worldly thirty-year-old middle-aged man, and the other was a nineteen-year-old young woman who had not seen much of the world. If they were to go off the rails, Leslie could pack up and go to who knows where.

But Ann Dvorak and the opinions of the general public in Hollywood did not stop the development of their romance. They initially agreed to shorten the one-year friendship trial period to six months because of Ann's mother's advice. But less than three months later, in a moment of impulse, they ran hand in hand to a small place in Arizona to get married. After they got married, they immediately returned to Hollywood to work. They worked hard day and night for five months, and then in another moment of impulse, they left Hollywood.

They took a boat from San Pedro Harbour in California to the south, passed through the Panama Canal to the east, and arrived in New York. This incident caused a sensation in Hollywood, because Ann Dvorak's contract had not yet expired when she ran away from Hollywood. And the next day, a new film was to be shot and everything was ready, but by the next day, Ann Dvorak was nowhere to be found. From New York, they ran to Europe, traveled in England for a long time, and then ran to Germany. Leslie Fenton made several films in Berlin. Ann Dvorak accompanied her husband to filming every day, and completely ignored her contract in Hollywood. When Leslie's filming was over, they took the opportunity to tour Southern Europe, passing through France, Italy, the Mediterranean, etc. to Africa. They were truly willful and indulgent, doing whatever they wanted, and had a great time playing for a total of nine months. Finally, they took a small boat back to America. They drifted at sea for as long as forty-eight days.

But this kind of travel was very beneficial to their marriage, because they had already jumped out of the atmosphere of the bad air in Hollywood. Their long-term travel had transformed them from an ordinary love union into inseparable companions who shared weal and woe. After they returned to Hollywood, the place where they lived, their daily life, everything was above the ordinary life there. They didn't like socialising and rarely attended banquets. They had their own separate life carved out by the two of them, so they could not be disturbed by the rumours of rumour-mongers at all. Of course, there were very sufficient reasons for their marriage to be able to maintain its happiness permanently.

Film Review

Review of "Charlie Chan's Greatest Case"

— Yiqun

Charlie Chan’s Greatest Case

｜Great Shanghai Screening｜

About two years ago, there was a film called "Charlie Chan's Detective Case" screened in Shanghai. Although the reporter did not get to see it, it seems that he still vaguely remembers that it caused a sensation for a while, and it seems that many people respected this detective king, Mr. Charlie Chan, because he could represent the Chinese or Orientals, and make a big splash and show off his skills in foreign lands. At least they were all very satisfied. Unfortunately, the reporter's eyes were too shallow, and he still has regrets!

This time, I was really lucky. Not only did I feast my eyes, but I also feasted my ears. After two years (?), the impression of Mr. Charlie Chan, which I had been missing, was vividly imprinted on my eyes and invaded my heart!

Like the Sherlock Holmes detective stories, Charlie Chan is a detective in a novel. Originally, the nationality of an ideal character can be freely cited by the author. What we should pay attention to now is the author's ideology, and how he understands and portrays this Chinese person.

What impressions does this "Charlie Chan's Greatest Case" give us? I can't help but sigh!

Let's put aside whether the current society's need for detectives and the detectives' tasks for the current society are correct. Let's not talk about these questions for now. Let's admit that the playwright's ideal is to attack the so-called laws and lawyers of the current society through Charlie Chan's detective skills. This point is of considerable significance. However, what great power does this have? Isn't it still just an ordinary love entanglement story? The ordinary love entanglement story selected such a fabricated theme, and the psychology of taking advantage of the topic is really obvious! Exposed without omission!

Now let's take a look at how the playwright portrays the Chinese Charlie Chan.

First, Charlie Chan is a person. Second, Charlie Chan's family is as disorderly and unorganized as a pigsty. Third, Charlie Chan's reproductive ability is high volume production, like pigs and dogs. Fourth, Charlie Chan is a miser. Fifth, the result of Charlie Chan's hard work in investigating the case is for a new car. Sixth, Charlie Chan is Chinese... Aren't these all vividly presented on paper? Charlie Chan is Chinese, that's all!

Isn't this an insult to the Chinese? Here, we can't help but admire the Americans' skill!

Our Announcement

— Ling He Moore

Since the advent of film criticism, it is an undeniable fact that Chinese films have been directly affected. Therefore, there are many rumours from the outside that some film entrepreneurs are trying to use film criticism to seek methods that are beneficial to the film business, etc.

Both of us are regular writers of film criticism. Whether or not this kind of bad phenomenon actually exists, we have the need to say a few words.

We will always strive for our own freedom. We are determined to maintain our own personality with a fair attitude. We will never be threatened or enticed by any party. We will always use the fairest words to criticize Chinese film works. | This is our oath. Please, pure and kind readers, strictly monitor us and criticize us. We are most grateful!

Carlton Screening of "Auspicious Land"

The Tianyi Film Company's new sound film "Auspicious Land" is one of the three sound films starring Chen Yumei in 1933, directed by Shao Zuiweng, and co-starring Tian Fang, Zhang Zhenduo, Ma Dongwu, and others. The plot depicts young farmers who sacrifice their own interests for the interests of the public, and country girls who do not succumb to the environment. At the same time, it also has considerable enlightenment on breaking superstitions and developing rural water conservancy education. The three Peking Opera excerpts interspersed in the film are especially wonderful. The film has been scheduled to be screened for the first time at the Carlton Grand Theatre in this city starting today, it is said.

The left is a scene from "Auspicious Land"

Audience Opinions

Thoughts After Watching "Salt Tide"

— Guang Dou

We have been looking forward to the screening of "Salt Tide" for a long time. Of course, it cannot be denied that this is a very interesting work. But I heard that: many powerful parts were cut off by the censorship authorities, which is very regrettable! As a result, those that were left after the cut and were released cannot deeply and powerfully imprint themselves on our hearts. However, the impression it gives us is at least unforgettable.

For example: the first step and the second step of the salt field... the hardship of the salt workers' work. Zhang Desan was arrested by the salt police and taken to the official's office. Young Master Hu's plan to occupy public land cut off the fuel for the salt workers. These are all things that can make the audience never forget.

The oppression of the petty salt workers by the local tyrants lacks powerful depiction, and the resistance of the salt workers is not very powerful either. In short, this is a mutilated film that has been cut, and it is worth watching to still have such consciousness. (Missing chapter but rewarded)

My Feelings About "Salt Tide"

— Yu Bi

"Salt Tide" is the first contribution of the Star Film Company this year.

The plot of this film tells us about the "liveliness" and "innocence" of country girls, the cunning of local tyrants and evil gentry, their "insidious treachery," the "loyalty" and reliability of old salt workers, their honest "purity," the romanticism of young masters, their "licentiousness," the "courageous" struggle of country salt workers, and the victory of "unity."

What does the director tell us in this film? He used all his strength to point out the "hardship" of the salt-making villagers, the means by which local tyrants and evil gentry "exploit" the salt workers. He also had considerable success in terms of technique. Compared with his past achievements, he has made amazing progress; but small flaws are always inevitable. For example, "A'feng" Your relative was detained on "suspicion" of burning illicit salt, but the reason for burning illicit salt was not stated.

Since "A'feng" hates "Xinwu," why did she agree to go to Shanghai with "Xinwu?" Isn't this "A'feng's" psychology too "contradictory?"

As for the actors, Hu Die's "A'feng" deserves our praise for her solemn attitude when "Xinwu" goes to seduce her. Wang Zhengxin's expression is also a success in this film. Gu Meijun's expression is as lively and charming as Hu Die's. Sun Min's expression also satisfies us. Wang Xianqi and Wang Mengshi both have good expressions.

Film, Novel, and Song World's Double Excellence The Cat and the Fiddle (5)

Mo Chen

Sally returned home and told Victor about it. Victor was silently pondering in front of the piano. He listened to Sally's words and said listlessly: "What's the use of that? My operetta is not finished yet. I can't finish it here either. I've tried so many times." Sally said: "Don't you like this place?" Victor hurriedly covered up and said: "This place is very good." But Sally had already seen it. She said: "I know you don't like this place." She was about to cry, but she tried her best to suppress herself. After a while, she said: "Okay, darling, let's go somewhere else... to a place where you can work quietly... um, I've got it... let's get married first. Then we'll go to the Riviera for our honeymoon. At that time, only I will be with you... no one else, and you can work and finish your operetta." After she finished speaking, she became happy again.

Victor took her hand and kissed her on the lips. He whispered: "Baby, I really can't think of anything in the world that would be better than being your husband. If I become your husband, I'll be happy to death every day. What I don't want is to be your guest forever, you know?" He wiped away her tears and continued: "As far as now, everything I eat, everything I wear, even this place, is all yours." Sally said: "Didn't we agree to be companions forever and share all the luck?" Victor complained to himself: "That's right, but what can I use to share with you? Do you want to share poverty with you?" Sally asked: "Don't you want to go back to Brussels?" Victor said that was where he started working before. Sally said: "Great, let's go back to Brussels, let's still live in that old house. Isn't that very interesting?" Victor thought of everything in the past, and was so happy that he couldn't speak for a while. He just kissed her on the lips frequently, telling her that she had made him happier than ever.

At this time, the guests downstairs had already gathered, and Victor hurriedly came down to greet the guests. Because he was so happy that he forgot himself, he hummed "Hi diddle dididle...The cat and the lio...The cow jumped over the moon..." as he went downstairs. Odette heard it and pulled her husband: "Darling, listen to how interesting that song is! Do you believe me, if I sing that song, it will cause a sensation again?" So she also hummed along with 'Hi diddle diddle'. Victor explained beside her: "This song is not finished yet, but it will be soon. We are going back to Brussels. Sally will go with me... in a few months..."

"Victor!" Doda rushed in from outside. He bowed and apologized to Odette on the one hand, and said to Victor on the other hand: "I have a word to tell you." So the two of them went to a corner together. Doda politely took out a cigarette case and offered it to Victor. Victor said: "Thank you, I don't smoke. What do you want to say?" Doda said: "It's about Sally. You are too sorry for her. She told me that she is going back to Brussels with you, isn't she?" Victor said: "Yes." (To be continued)
